The Banking Crisis Has Passed

Roosevelt Announces that American Banks Will Reopen Today 47

Sound Banks Will Be Fully Open by Wednesday

Federal Reserve Banks Supply Currency to All Banks

▲Washington, 11th (Dispatch) U.S. President Roosevelt announced today that national banks will gradually reopen starting Monday. It is hoped that solid banks will be fully operational by Wednesday. Licenses are scheduled to be issued on Monday to all solid banks under the Federal Reserve System. Licenses will be issued on Tuesday to sound banks in various cities that have joined formal clearinghouses. On Wednesday, licenses will be issued to all other banks that can prove their foundation is solid. The second category can actually include all important banks that do not join the Federal Reserve System, as there are currently 250 cities and towns in the United States that have organized clearinghouses. Today, the twelve Federal Reserve Banks have, in accordance with the order of Treasury Secretary Woodin, sent currency to various banks so that they can operate their full business after opening. Only transactions in gold, both domestic and foreign, are prohibited.

▲Washington, 11th (Dispatch) Tonight, Treasury Secretary Woodin issued a further order, slightly altering the regulations for the bank reopening period. Only member banks of the Federal Reserve System and Federal Reserve Banks located in the same city can reopen on Monday. As for other member banks located in other cities, they and the member banks of clearinghouses will open on the next day. The reason is that the Federal Reserve Banks will not be able to send currency to banks in other cities before Monday. Therefore, only banks in twelve cities, including New York, Chicago, Cleveland, San Francisco, Philadelphia, Boston, Kansas City, Atlanta, Richmond, St. Louis, Dallas, and Minneapolis, will open on Monday.

Government Handling 48

President Roosevelt, who at this time holds nationwide financial dictatorial powers, has announced that he will broadcast a summary of the events of the past few days to the entire nation over the radio at 10 p.m. on Sunday night so that everyone can have a clear understanding. He also stated that the technical difficulties in all banking plans have been eliminated, and various banks will start to reopen starting Monday. At the same time, the Treasury Department reported that the return of privately hoarded money to banks is continuing to increase sharply. As of tonight, it has reached 1 billion yuan, which is approximately equal to the amount withdrawn in the two days before the President's proclamation amending the bank holiday. The Treasury Department is confident that the banking industry will proceed smoothly from now on, so it has announced the government's spring debt exchange plan, which will begin on Monday with the submission of 800 million yuan in Treasury bonds for bank subscription to repay maturing debts. It is expected that this money will be raised quickly, or that the amount of subscriptions will even exceed the amount of issuance.

Bank Preparations 49

At this time, national banks are actively surveying and settling accounts in the hope of demonstrating their full ability to pay so that they can reopen. It is said that the vast majority can meet this qualification. It is expected that after the banks open, there will be sufficient solid institutions in various places to handle all financial matters. It is reported that various banks in San Francisco have reported to the Treasury Department that they can comply with the most stringent regulations set by the government. Other major cities have also made similar reports. Banks in Hawaii, Texas, and Kansas have announced that they are ready to open on Monday. Eastern banks have also demonstrated that their foundations are solid and that they are prepared to reopen quickly. The Treasury Department has now notified various banks that they may also accept checks issued before March 6, but only for transfer, not for cash payments. The Treasury Department is determined not to allow currency to fall into the hands of those making runs on banks. It was recently heard that the government has decided to divide the banks into three categories and reopen them on different days purely for convenience because various banks must have huge amounts of currency before they can open, but transportation takes time.

Securities Trading 50

New York, 11th (Dispatch) The board of directors of the New York Stock Exchange decided today that it will still not open next Monday. According to sources in the exchange, it will probably open on Wednesday because it is of little value for the exchange to open when banks in other cities have not fully resumed operations. As for the offices of various brokers, various order forms continue to be sent in an endless stream because it is expected that securities will rise in price after the opening.

Budget Cuts Passed 51

Washington, 11th (Dispatch) At this time, although the President and the Treasury Secretary have made solid progress in handling the banking crisis, they have encountered difficulties in Congress because a majority of Democratic congressmen opposed the President's proposed free reduction of veterans' pensions, disobeying party orders and not adhering to the constraints of the party conference. The President plans to reduce the pensions of non-disabled veterans by half, while those who generally support veterans' interests are trying to revive and pass the Blandoning Amendment, which would limit the reduction to no more than one-quarter. Finally, after appeals from House Speaker Rayburn and various Democratic leaders, the Republican faction supporting the budget cuts supported the proposal, and the entire budget cut proposal was passed according to the government's original proposal by a vote of 266 to 138. Dissecting the opponents, there were 91 Democrats, 42 Republicans, and 5 Farmer-Labor Party members. After the proposal was passed in the House, it was immediately transferred to the Senate. The Senate Finance Committee then convened immediately and passed the original proposal. It is now expected that the Senate will vote on Monday. After the House passed the proposal, the Senate adjourned to express condolences because Republican Senator Howell passed away from lung disease here this afternoon. Howell was sixty-eight years old and had always advocated for the public ownership of public utilities.

The Second and Third Internationals Join Hands 52

(Basel, 11th (Dispatch)) According to Moscow sources, the Soviet Communist Party's Third International is seeking to contact the Socialist Second International to make a joint struggle because of the German government's anti-communist policies. The Swiss Communist Party has formally requested the Socialist Party to make a joint demonstration. It is reported that the Socialist Party has agreed. According to London sources, the British Communist Party has also made a similar application to the Labour Party, but it has been rejected by the Labour Party.

(Berlin, 11th (Dispatch)) The police authorities heard that a Hungarian communist leader who has lived in Russia for a long time and one German leader have secretly arrived here, hoping to incite unrest. Today, the images of the two men have been disseminated everywhere.

Recent Soviet Foreign Policy (Authored by Molotov) 53

Furthermore, the termination of the 1930 Anglo-Soviet trade agreement also warrants discussion. This agreement was terminated by the British government, and its true purpose remains unknown. However, speculating, if the intention was to intimidate the Soviet Union by severing the trade agreement, that would be rash, as the Soviet Union is not afraid. And if the intention was to inflict some kind of loss on the Soviet Union, that would be even more miscalculated. Anyone who needs to order from the Soviet Union understands this. We are well aware that countries with regular diplomatic and trade relations with the Soviet Union benefit more than others. In particular, unlike some capitalist countries, the Soviet Union always fully fulfills its obligations on time and never breaches contracts or defaults on debts.

Speaking of which, one cannot help but mention the basic mission of Soviet foreign policy: to implement a policy of peace. The Soviet Union pays close attention to issues related to guaranteeing general peace or related to a second world war. The Soviet Union's proposal for a general and genuine disarmament plan in February of last year was simply an expression of this intention.

The Soviet government's proposal to many countries to conclude non-aggression treaties is also a manifestation of its struggle for the peace policy it upholds. In the past year alone, the Soviet Union has made great progress in concluding non-aggression pacts. The signing and ratification of non-aggression treaties by the governments of Poland, Finland, Estonia, and Lithuania is a great victory for Soviet diplomacy. These non-aggression treaties are of great significance for consolidating the cause of peace. The Soviet Union and France have also signed a non-aggression treaty, but this matter is still unfinished because France has not yet ratified the treaty. (Translator's note: The Franco-Soviet treaty has already been ratified.)

However, the Soviet Union's relationship with Romania is slightly different. Romania has refused to sign a non-aggression treaty with the Soviet Union. Therefore, in the West, only one country bordering the Soviet Union has refused to sign a non-aggression pact. There is no need to examine this issue in detail; it is only necessary to point out that Romania's refusal to conclude a non-aggression treaty with the Soviet Union is not due to any opinion of the Romanian government itself on this issue, but rather to external reasons. It is extremely wrong for political dictionaries to include such countries, which in fact have no independent foreign policy but are subordinate to the foreign policy of another strong country, among so-called "independent" countries. In any case, the victims of this are only Romania and its government. Now, let us turn to the Far East issue.

The League of Nations' handling of the Far East issue is well known throughout the world. It has been more than a year since the League of Nations accepted the Manchurian Incident. There have been several resolutions on this issue. The League of Nations has also discussed the situation in China and Manchuria many times and has sent a special investigation committee to investigate the area. The committee's report has also been published for a long time and has returned to Europe to report. The League of Nations has established an extra committee on this issue, and then another committee. Its resolutions are also the most comprehensive possible. However, there has been no progress whatsoever. Only one thing has progressed very quickly, and that is the League of Nations' credibility in the eyes of the world, which has been increasingly discredited.

The Soviet Union has never linked its hopes with the League of Nations and its committees, but the issue of international relations in the Far East is extremely important to the Soviet Union. Therefore, it has had to take many measures.

Considering the complicated environment in the Far East, the Soviet government proposed to Japan a year ago to conclude a non-aggression treaty. In the current international environment, the political significance of this move is very obvious and need not be elaborated. However, the Japanese government soon notified the Soviet government that the time was not yet ripe for the conclusion of this agreement. There is no need to analyze in detail the reasons for the Japanese government's rejection of the Soviet government's proposal to conclude a non-aggression pact. We know that this rejection is indeed temporary, but we must also consider the facts.

The Soviet government strictly adheres to a policy of neutrality in the Far East, and it still firmly adheres to this position and will continue to implement this policy to the end. However, the attitude of a few Japanese political figures towards the Soviet Union has recently become noticeable. For example, the Japanese military has spread provocative news about the Soviet government and the future Soviet ambassador to China. Regardless of the fact that the Soviet government has firmly denied these anti-Soviet rumors, Japanese Foreign Minister Uchida reiterated the old trick in his speech to the Japanese parliament on January 21.

These anti-Soviet rumors collapse on their own and do not need to be refuted. As for the restoration of Sino-Soviet diplomatic relations, the Soviet government resolves this issue regardless of who benefits and who does not. It knows that it is based on the interests of general peace and its own peace policy.

Uchida declared in the Japanese Diet that since the Manchurian Incident, no unpleasant incidents have occurred in Soviet-Japanese relations because the Soviet government has maintained a "cautious stance." This should be especially pointed out: the issue is not that Soviet policy is cautious; this policy is not only cautious but also carefully considered. The starting point for the Soviet government is based on the interests of general peace and the consolidation of external peace interests. Regardless of how other countries evaluate this peace policy, the Soviet government will resolutely implement it in its foreign relations to the end.

The international environment also reminds the Soviet Union to be deeply vigilant, especially the need to pay special attention to the situation in the Far East. This must be reflected in all work and all construction endeavors. In 1933, there must be greater progress in socialist construction because the consolidation of the Soviet Union's internal and external situation depends entirely on the victory of its economic work. (To be continued)

Feng Yuxiang Advocates Strenuous Counter-Offensive 54

Demands Yuguan and Rehe be Recovered Soonest; Zhangjiakou Equals the Frontline, Ready for a Fight

Zhangjiakou Correspondence: The reporter arrived in Zhangjiakou on the Ping-Sui train on the 6th. The next morning at about 8 o'clock, I went to the library on Tuergou South Street, east of the station, to visit Mr. Feng Yuxiang. Two guards with broadswords stood guard at the door, amiable and kind. Seeing the reporter arrive, they first raised their hands in salute. After inquiring about my intention, they passed my card in. Soon, two young men came out to greet me. I learned their names were Jin Qingyu and Li Zhongyi, and they were very hospitable. After I explained my intention, they replied that Mr. (i.e., Mr. Feng) was currently teaching and had no time to meet. I asked when he would be free, and they replied at 5:00 p.m. I asked how Mr. Feng was doing recently. They said that Mr. Feng gets up at 6:00 a.m. and starts his daily lessons at 8:00 a.m., such as English, Sinology, political economy, and social sciences, and also practices calligraphy, painting, growing vegetables, and walking. The time is from 8:00 a.m. to 12:00 p.m., and from 1:00 p.m. to 5:00 p.m. He declines all social engagements and rarely goes out. After the Yuguan Incident, Mr. Feng sent his family to another place, striving to think quietly. Whenever I see him in his spare time after class, patting his thigh and wielding a sword, I can see his deep concern for the country. The reporter then left and returned at 5:00 p.m., when Mr. Feng agreed to meet me. Mr. Feng wore cloth cotton clothes and trousers, a fur-lined blue cloth overcoat, and old-fashioned cotton shoes. After entering the living room, he took off his overcoat, with a warm smile and full of energy. He said repeatedly, "Sir, you have come such a long way in this cold weather to see me. I am too unworthy." The reporter explained the purpose of his visit to Zhangjiakou, and he answered sincerely. The record of his conversation is as follows: "Now the enemy is invading us, step by step, closer and closer. We have no way to survive except to resist. At this time, to deal with the current situation, we should be clear about right and wrong, and distinguish black and white. For example, Tang Yulin abandoned Chengde without a fight. Not only should the government strictly arrest and punish him, but the people should also automatically rise up and chop him. If not, how can we show the national spirit of the Nineteenth Route Army's sacrifice for the country? And there is no truth in the world. I advocate that all of Tang Yulin's property should be confiscated to subsidize the anti-Japanese military expenses or to relieve the refugees in Rehe Province. Now the enemy is approaching us, and we must strive to counter-attack. Yuguan and Rehe must be recovered as soon as possible. We need to fight several more fierce battles. Even if we lose the battle, we will leave behind a national spirit that will last forever. Seeing that we are about to become slaves of a conquered nation, the people of the whole country should quickly rise up to resist Japan. Those who resist Japan are good friends, and those who do not resist Japan are traitors. At this time, we must all rise up together to overthrow the traitors who do not resist Japan. I believe that at this time of national crisis, all kinds of groups should be able to say what they want to say. People's groups should strengthen their forces. The power of the people is the most important thing to save the country. Furthermore, speaking of my going to Nanjing, now that the enemy is in the north, I have no need to go south. And there is a rumor that I am going to Taiyuan. The enemy is now in the east, so why should I go west? After the September 18th Incident, I have always advocated using force to recover the lost territories. People should have self-knowledge and measure their own virtue and ability. I am really not qualified to lead people to do it. Now Zhangjiakou is also the front line. I still have two guns. I can shoot with both my left and right hands. And with my comrades, I will definitely be able to fight to the death with them. Finally, I hope that the people will strengthen their forces to stand on the front line, and I will stand in the middle of this front line," and so on. Later, the reporter asked if Li Xiehe had come to see Mr. Feng. He replied that Li was about to come and showed a telegram he had received that day. The reporter then bid farewell. (7th)

A Bird's-Eye View of Chahar 55

Japanese Residents in Zhangjiakou Have Left; People are Carrying Out Patriotic Movements; Business Circles Eagerly Await Sino-Mongolian Trade

Zhangjiakou Correspondence: Since the Japanese army invaded and occupied Chengde, the Japanese army has intended to peek into Chahar Province. Therefore, the position of Chahar Province is becoming increasingly important. I will record the recent situation of Chahar Province as follows for the attention of the people of the country.

The northeast of Chahar Province borders Rehe. Duolun Nuoer (i.e., Duolun County) in the north faces Linyao in Rehe, and is a passage into Rehe. Therefore, Rehe and Chahar provinces have a relationship of interdependence. Whether Chahar Province can be preserved depends on Rehe. Now the Japanese residents in Zhangjiakou have completely left Chahar and returned to their country. The Japanese consulate in Zhangjiakou is also preparing to lower its flag and withdraw to Beiping. Chahar Province is an important route to Kulun. When Sino-Mongolian trade was conducted in the past, merchants gathered in Zhangjiakou and Duolun, and commerce was concentrated. Since the cessation of Sino-Mongolian trade, Zhangjiakou's commerce has declined sharply, and it has not yet returned to its former glory. Chahar Province has a total of sixteen counties, which is equal to the number of counties in Rehe and Suiyuan. The population is more than 460,000 people. The province's annual income is 3 million yuan, which is not enough for government expenses. Therefore, after the national implementation of cutting taxes in the 19th year of the Republic, Chahar Province was the only province that did not implement cutting taxes due to financial difficulties. To this day, what Chahar Province relies on to maintain the situation is taxes. Education in Chahar Province has developed greatly recently, but the people's thinking is stubborn and has the style of Mongolians. There are a total of six middle schools and normal schools in the province. People's education is also quite developed. Chahar Province has no major production. Several northern counties border Outer Mongolia and produce furs and skins. The people's staple food is oil noodles. The province produces millet and wheat, which can be used for the province and can also be transported to Hebei. The province is mostly mountainous, and the climate is severely cold. In March and April of spring, people still wear leather clothes. Since Rehe issued a warning, the people of Chahar Province have also organized an anti-Japanese association. It has now united all sectors of the party, government, military, academia, and business, and has begun to carry out patriotic movements, and is raising funds to comfort the anti-Japanese soldiers at the front and to comfort the families of the soldiers who died in battle. Since Feng Yuxiang went to Zhangjiakou from Taian in October of last year, he has gone to the library in his residence and closed the door to read books. He has repeatedly expressed his determination to resist Japan. According to Feng, if the central government is determined to resist Japan, he himself, even if he is a soldier carrying a gun, will be happy to kill the enemy in the vanguard. This shows that Feng does not choose a position on the issue of resisting Japan and is willing to share his determination with the central government. Feng also said that whether or not to go to Nanjing is not a problem. The anti-Japanese work is not in the region, which shows his frankness. Since China and Russia restored diplomatic relations, Sino-Mongolian merchants have begun to travel back and forth. Chinese merchants in Kulun are no longer treated harshly by the Outer Mongolian government. Any Chinese merchant with a passport can enter the country. Before Sino-Mongolian trade officially began, the German company Dehua Foreign Firm contracted Sino-Mongolian trade affairs for one year. The foreign firm is located in Zhangjiakou. In the past year, the trade with Kulun amounted to 5 million yuan in Chinese currency. The goods transported to Outer Mongolia were mainly Shandong silk, brick tea, leather boots, stirrups, and domestic cloth. The goods imported from Outer Mongolia were mainly furs, crystals, mushrooms, and deer antlers. The automobiles between Zhangjiakou and Kulun can now travel unimpeded. After the implementation of trade with Outer Mongolia, not only will the commerce of Chahar and Suiyuan provinces be able to turn around, but also the commerce of North China will be able to develop. Therefore, the business community here is eagerly awaiting the official resumption of Sino-Mongolian trade as soon as possible, so as not to be contracted by foreign firms.

Jiang Zuobin Discusses the Trend of Sino-Japanese Relations 56

It Was Expected That the League of Nations Would Not Sanction Japan; There May Be New Paths Discovered by Going North to Meet Chiang

Beijing News: Minister to Japan Jiang Zuobin arrived in Beijing by the Shanghai-Nanjing night train early (11th) morning at eight o'clock. After getting off the train, he went to his private residence in Shatangyuan to rest. He will go north to meet Chairman Chiang within a few days to report everything. Mr. Jiang made the following remarks to those who visited him:

The Future of Sino-Japanese Relations is Worrying 57

Question: The Japanese army's occupation of Rehe has made the future of Sino-Japanese relations even worse. What does the gentleman think is the plan to save the situation? Answer: Resistance is of course legitimate self-defense, but judging from the resistance situation in Rehe, our army retreated without a fight. However, the future prospects for the situation with Japan are very worrying. Moreover, Japan sees that it has acquired Rehe so easily, which was initially unexpected. The desires of ambitious people will be even greater. Therefore, it is difficult to say at this time whether the Japanese army in China will be able to declare a conclusion after occupying Rehe. And seeing that it is so easy to occupy Chinese territory, it is common sense to gain an inch and then seek a yard. Question: Then will Suiyuan and Chahar, which border Rehe, be in frequent danger? Answer: When I left Japan to return to China, I had not yet received news of the Japanese army's attack on Chahar and Suiyuan. However, whether the Japanese army in North China can stop military operations at this time depends on whether our country can resist and the degree of resistance.

League of Nations Sanctions Japan 58

Question: Since the League of Nations does not implement sanctions against violent Japan, and our country's resistance situation is like this, what will happen to Japan in the end? Answer: It was not until today that I knew that the League of Nations could not sanction Japan. It was already in my mind long ago. China's own affairs, hoping for the assistance of the League of Nations, the starting point is only a reliance. Therefore, the hope for the League of Nations was originally a kind of hope that was secondary, not the only one. The main thing lies in the determination of the whole country to resist with perseverance and the spirit of striving for self-improvement. Now that the League of Nations does not sanction Japan, we do not need to be too disappointed. In the end, we will be able to be self-aware and fight. There is still something to tell, that is, do not passively hope that Japan will fall by itself, only actively strive for self-improvement in China. Question: There is a lot of talk about the Anglo-Japanese alliance. What is the truth? Answer: The Anglo-Japanese alliance has not yet reached a completely mature stage. What the outside world is saying may also be an exaggerated inference. Question: The United Kingdom advocates banning the sale of arms to China and Japan. This is undoubtedly indirect assistance to Japan. We therefore have doubts about the Anglo-Japanese alliance. Answer: The United Kingdom's advocacy of banning the sale of arms to China and Japan is of great importance to our country, but the impact on Japan is very small because Japan is a newly emerging industrial country, and everything is fully prepared.

There Will Eventually Be a New Path 59

Question: Then under the pressure of Japanese aggression, what policy can our country use to survive? Answer: Since the League of Nations does not sanction Japan, and the resistance situation in Rehe is like this, the future of China is very worrying. However, there will eventually be a new path. It must not be like walking on the road, so that there is no way to go. Question: What is the new path that the gentleman is talking about? Answer: I have no preconceived notions about this. I must go north to see Chairman Chiang within a few days, and then the central government and Chairman Chiang will decide on a countermeasure. Question: I heard that the gentleman has returned to China this time with a major mission on Sino-Japanese relations. I don't know if it is true. Answer: After receiving the telegram, I left Japan and returned to China. I cannot bear the so-called major mission. The issue of Japan will be decided by the central government. Question: How many months of leave does the gentleman have? Answer: There is no fixed vacation. After going north within a few days, our country's decision-making on Japan will be clear.

Japanese Troops in Wuhan Create Disturbances 60

Salt Police Open Fire to Seize Smugglers, Japanese Troops Act as if Facing a Great Enemy

Hankou Correspondence: When the war in Rehe first started, the Japanese troops stationed in Wuhan actively made military deployments and intended to provoke. When our side maintained calmness, the Japanese had no chance to take advantage of, and the situation gradually eased. However, they are still secretly seizing the opportunity to move. The tight security of the Japanese concession and the reconnaissance of Japanese warships back and forth are no different from when things were tense. Recently, there are four Japanese warships stationed in Wuhan: Atago, Tsushima, Atami, and Hira, with a total of more than 1,000 marines. Commander Sakano of the 3rd Overseas Dispatch Fleet is stationed on the Atago flagship to command. On the evening of the 10th, the marines of the Tsushima ship caused trouble due to a misunderstanding because the salt bureau police opened fire to seize smugglers. It was not explained until the morning of the 11th. It turned out that the anti-smuggling battalion under the jurisdiction of the Hubei Shore Salt Bureau Inspection Office sent teams of soldiers to secretly investigate various wharves in the city in order to investigate and seize smuggled salt. At about 9 p.m. on the 10th, the soldiers of the battalion discovered several boats on the river in front of Eleven Pier 3 carrying salt to smuggle. Because the boats refused to approach the shore, they fired two shots, intending to scare them into submission. After the Japanese warship Tsushima, which was moored on the river at the intersection of the Japanese special zone, discovered the gunfire, it immediately ordered the marines to land fully armed and deploy in the Japanese concession, as if facing a great enemy, and sent plainclothes detectives to investigate our actions. At that time, Chen Haiqing, the director of the Eleven Pier, reported the truth of the shooting to the Japanese military authorities by telephone through the president of the Tongren Hospital nearby. The marines of the ship withdrew to the ship at 2 a.m. on the 11th. The Wuhan Garrison Command stated that the General Headquarters and the Pacification Commissioner's Office had long expressly prohibited arbitrary shooting in the garrison area. The current situation is serious, and it is even more impermissible to deliberately violate the prohibition and disrupt order and tranquility. It immediately sent a letter to the Salt Bureau Inspection Office to severely punish the tax police who fired without authorization and presented the situation to the General Headquarters and the Pacification Commissioner's Office for review and approval, and requested a reaffirmation of the prohibition to ensure security. In addition, the Japanese concession held a conscription inspection on the 10th, and all those of conscription age returned to their country. It is said that there was also a disturbance, but the details are unknown. (March 11)

Civil Service Appointment Law 61

The Civil Service Appointment Law promulgated by the National Government on the 11th is as follows:

(Article 1) The appointment of civil servants shall be governed by this law, unless otherwise provided by law. (Article 2) Civil servants in the selected appointment rank shall be appointed from those who have one of the following qualifications: (1) Those who are currently or have been in the selected appointment rank and have passed screening and review or performance evaluation; (2) Those who are currently or have been in the highest recommended appointment rank for more than two years and have passed screening and review or performance evaluation; (3) Those who have served as political officials for more than one year; (4) Those who have made special contributions to the Republic of China or have devoted themselves to the National Revolution for more than ten years and have made contributions; (5) Those who have special writings or inventions in academics. (Article 3) Civil servants in the recommended appointment rank shall be appointed from those who have one of the following qualifications: (1) Those who have passed the higher examination or the special examination equivalent to the higher examination; (2) Those who are currently or have been in the recommended appointment rank and have passed screening and review or performance evaluation; (3) Those who are currently or have been in the highest delegated appointment rank for more than three years and have passed screening and review or performance evaluation; (4) Those who have made contributions to the Republic of China or have devoted themselves to the National Revolution for more than seven years and have made achievements; (5) Those who have graduated from universities at home and abroad recognized by the Ministry of Education and have specialized writings that have passed review. (Article 4) Civil servants in the delegated appointment rank shall be appointed from those who have one of the following qualifications: (1) Those who have passed the ordinary examination or the special examination equivalent to the ordinary examination; (2) Those who are currently or have been in the delegated appointment rank and have passed screening and review or performance evaluation; (3) Those who have been employed for more than three years and have excellent performance; (4) Those who have devoted themselves to the National Revolution for more than five years and have made achievements; (5) Those who have graduated from schools above the specialized school level. (Article 5) The appointment of civil servants shall, in addition to the provisions of the preceding three articles, be limited to those whose academic qualifications, positions, experience, and the duties of the position they hold are equivalent. (Article 6) Those who have one of the following circumstances shall not be appointed as civil servants: (1) Those who have been deprived of civil rights and have not yet been restored; (2) Those who have embezzled public funds and have not yet repaid them; (3) Those who have been punished for embezzlement; (4) Those who use opium or its substitutes. (Article 7) The appointment of civil servants in the selected appointment rank and the recommended appointment rank shall be appointed separately by the National Government after being reviewed and qualified by the Ministry of Personnel; the appointment of civil servants in the delegated appointment rank shall be appointed by the competent official after being reviewed and qualified by the Ministry of Personnel. After receiving the documents in the preceding two paragraphs, the Ministry of Personnel shall immediately submit them for review and decide whether they are qualified or unqualified. (Article 8) During the period of requesting a selected appointment, presenting a recommended appointment, or proposing a delegated appointment, the competent official may appoint a person with corresponding qualifications as an agent when necessary, but the term of agency shall not exceed three months. (Article 9) Those who have passed the examination shall be assigned to corresponding official agencies for appointment according to the type and subject of the examination. (Article 10) Civil servants in the recommended appointment rank and the delegated appointment rank shall be appointed from those who have passed the examination as soon as possible. The appointment of those who have passed the examination shall be in the order of distribution by the Ministry of Personnel. (Article 11) The appointment procedure shall be divided into trial appointment and actual appointment. Those who have completed one year of trial appointment may be actually appointed. (Article 12) Newly appointed personnel shall be given a trial appointment and shall be appointed from the lowest grade salary. However, those who have been civil servants and have accumulated seniority and merit may be given a salary according to their original grade. Those who have the qualifications for a selected appointment but are appointed to a recommended appointment or who have the qualifications for a recommended appointment but are appointed to a delegated appointment shall not be subject to the provisions of the preceding paragraph and shall retain their original qualifications. (Article 13) This law shall not apply to political officials. (Article 14) In order to implement this law, the Ministry of Personnel may separately formulate regulations and submit them to the Examination Yuan for transfer to the National Government for approval. (Article 15) The date of implementation of this law shall be determined by order.

Wuxi

Eighth Anniversary of the Death of the Premier 62

At about 10 a.m. yesterday, the county party headquarters of this county specially convened representatives from various institutions, groups, and schools in the grand hall to hold a memorial service for the eighth anniversary of the death of the Premier. More than 300 people attended. Chairman Xu Chizi presided over the ceremony. After the ceremony, the chairman reported on the Premier's revolutionary career and the need to continue his legacy in the future, and urged the government to resist foreign aggression. Then, representatives of various institutions and groups gave speeches, which were full of encouragement and moved the listeners.

Police Arrest Five Robbers 63

Last month, the family of Lu Agen, a villager in Zhuma Bridge, the 13th district of the county, had several stones of white rice robbed by villagers. It was not until recently that it was discovered that the robbers were Chen Gensheng, Zhou Agou, Gu Apei, Chen Genlin, and Chen Afu, who lived nearby. The police team stationed in the village were informed and arrested Chen Gensheng and the other five people and presented them to the county government. Yesterday, they were transferred to the county court. After the hearing by Prosecutor Shen, he ordered them to be detained together to await further interrogation and handling.

Nantong

Tonghai Railway Temporarily Difficult to Build 64

In order to develop transportation in the coastal area of Jiangbei, the provincial government specially planned to build the Tonghai Railway, from Nantong to Haizhou. The route has been commissioned to engineer Wang Shixi and others to survey and complete. It was originally scheduled to start construction in March, but it has been decided to postpone construction temporarily due to lack of funds.

Planning to Compile Coastal Patrol Team 65

The fishing season is approaching in various coastal areas of Jiangbei. However, sea bandits and mutinying soldiers are causing trouble on the sea. The coastal counties of Tongtai have decided to follow the provincial order and jointly compile a water patrol team to protect fishermen and prevent bandits. Planning is underway.

Gaoyou

Record of Kidnapping and Robbery Cases 66

Seven bandits suddenly came to the home of Zhang Yushsheng, a farmer in Zhangjiaxia, the ninth district of the county, the night before last. Each of them held long and short guns and broke into the bedroom to search wildly. Because there was not much in the house, they kidnapped Zhang and told his family to prepare 1,000 yuan in silver to redeem him, otherwise they would burn and kill him. In addition, the home of Chen Huanzhang, the chief of Beiwang Township in the district, was also searched and robbed by bandits that night. It is said that the loss was more than 500 yuan.

Three Deaths in Devastating Fire at Duan Duo 67

In Duan Duo Township, under this county's jurisdiction, the widowed Madam Gu Feng, at around 9 o'clock the night before last, was smoking her dry tobacco in bed. Embers fell onto the bedding, causing a fire. In an instant, the fire illuminated the sky. Although neighbors tried their utmost to extinguish the blaze, the flames were too intense to be put out. By the time the fire was extinguished, all the houses had been reduced to ashes. Only one daughter escaped. Madam Gu Feng and her two sons all perished in the fire, a truly tragic event.

Shaoxing

Local Branch Court Seal Stolen 68

At the Shaoxing Local Branch Court, a serious case occurred on the morning of the 11th. The court seal was stolen. Chief Judge Jiang Bingkui immediately issued an emergency order to close the iron gates at both entrances. All parties, except those directly involved in legal proceedings or those with special reasons, were barred from entering or leaving. A rigorous investigation of all court personnel was undertaken.

Security Guard Commits Suicide by Gunshot 69

Xie Fukang, a security guard in the temporary cadre team of the Shaoxing Da Shan Temple security force, committed suicide because his fiancée disliked his poverty and showed a strong unwillingness to marry him. This caused him mental distress, and he lost his composure. Yesterday, in his dormitory upstairs, he shot himself with a rifle. The bullet struck his navel, and he fell to the ground, dying instantly.

Two Banks Scheduled to Open 70

In addition to the four banks already in Shaoxing—Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Central Bank, and Farmers and Workers Bank—two more banks are scheduled to open. One is the Shaoxing Local Farmers Bank, scheduled to open on the 24th, and the other is the Shaoxing Branch of the Zhejiang Local Bank, scheduled to open on the 16th.

Xiaoshan

Large Number of Refugees Escorted Out of Territory 71

More than a hundred refugees from Hunan arrived in Xiaosi Bu, eastern Xiaoshan, the other day, supporting the old and carrying the young, in a very miserable state. On the morning of the 11th, they begged for food along the road from Guali Jiudunfang. The Guali Township police temporarily collected several yuan in silver and rice for them and escorted them to Anchang to leave the territory, so the area did not suffer disturbances. It is reported that another group came from Shanwan, forcibly demanding food from households in Shenglin villages, behaving barbarically. Residents all closed their doors. Fortunately, the township office sent local guards to distribute rice on their behalf, and they then left the territory.

Robbery with Injury Outside the South Gate 72

On the night of the 10th, five robbers speaking a foreign dialect suddenly entered the Zheng family's residence near Sheqian outside the South Gate. They opened the front door and went straight in, ransacking boxes and chests upstairs. They robbed four gold rings, seven silk garments, and two strings of pearls. When the family's nine-year-old daughter cried out, one of the robbers cut her face with a knife. The victim has reported the incident to the county and requested an arrest.

Hangzhou

Four Young Men and Women Commit Suicide 73

At 5 p.m. on the 11th, on the hillside of Jiuyao Mountain, opposite Chishan Bu in West Lake, four young men and women were found to have committed suicide by poison. Their deaths were gruesome. The local police station reported the incident to the Hangzhou District Court. This afternoon, Court Prosecutor Zhu Henghua, accompanied by Coroner Feng Shengxiang, went to conduct an examination. The four young people wore badges from the Anhui Provincial Fourth Middle School. One of the males was about 23 or 24 years old, and the other was about 20 years old. The older one wore a dark student uniform with a woolen overcoat, and the younger one wore a cotton robe over a blue cloth long gown. When their clothes were removed, they each wore a sports undershirt with the red characters "Wan Hun" (Anhui Soul) and "Chong Xiao" (Soaring Ambition) respectively. Both girls wore gray cloth qipaos with cloth jackets. All four had foam in their mouths, and their teeth and nails were black. The cause of the suicide is unknown. A thorough search of their belongings revealed only a pencil on one of the girls. In the pocket of the male student wearing the blue robe was a notice from the Anhui Provincial Fourth Middle School to the parents of student He Jiazhang informing them of his expulsion, along with a ship ticket for the Yihe Company in Anqing and a few small silver and copper coins. General speculation is that the four students were classmates at Anhui Fourth Middle School. Due to a romantic entanglement, they neglected their studies and were expelled. They came to Hangzhou after many twists and turns and, due to financial difficulties, this tragic event occurred.

Letter

Letter from Tan Yigui 74

To the esteemed editor: I have read the report in the Changshu News section of your newspaper on March 11th, which states that County Magistrate Tan was accused and had some differences of opinion with the head of the Security Corps, a Mr. Lu. It said that he had gone to the provincial capital yesterday to consult on everything and had requested a transfer, etc. This is completely untrue. I am deeply concerned that this will cause readers to misunderstand. I am writing this letter to correct the record and clarify the truth. Sincerely, Tan Yigui

Local News

Zhang Xueliang Arrives in Shanghai by Plane Yesterday 75

Song Ziwen, Dai Ji, and Others Personally Welcome Him, Waiting for Yu Fengzhi to Arrive Before Traveling Abroad Together; Zhang Expresses Hope That Society Will Treat Him as an Ordinary Citizen

After Zhang Xueliang telegraphed his resignation in Beiping, he left Beiping by his private Ford airplane yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, accompanied by his secretary Li Yingchao, advisor Donald, and others, and came to Shanghai. Yesterday afternoon at 3:10 PM, they safely arrived at Hongqiao Airport. Song Ziwen, Dai Ji, Wu Tiecheng, and the American Consul General Mr. Cunninghan, and others all went to welcome him. After Mr. Zhang disembarked, he went with Song Ziwen in the same car to the Song residence on Qizhi Road for a brief rest. Around 6:00 PM, he returned to his temporary residence at No. 181 Fuxu Road, waiting for his wife to arrive in Shanghai before traveling abroad together. Mr. Zhang issued a simple written statement last night, saying that he has already resigned from his post and hopes that society will treat him as an ordinary citizen. He no longer has any opinions on state affairs that can be stated, etc. The details are recorded below:

Chinese and Western Figures Welcome Him 76

Yesterday afternoon, various dignitaries in Shanghai, hearing that Zhang Xueliang was coming south, went to the airport one after another around noon to welcome him. Those who arrived included Acting President of the Executive Yuan Song Ziwen, Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Songhu Garrison Commander Dai Ji, Jianghai Customs Superintendent Tang Haian, Director of the Shanghai Security Bureau Yang Hu, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government Yu Hongjun, Secretary of the Ministry of Finance Guo Dehua and his wife, Huang Chun Tao, Director of the Public Security Bureau Wen Hongen, Song Ziliang, Song Zian, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Hu Junzhuang, Dong Xian Guang, Fu Xiao An, the American Consul General Mr. Cunninghan and his wife, representative of the Salt Administration, Dr. Gale and his wife, and dozens of others. The Public Security Bureau also sent a military band to the airport to welcome him.

Strict Security at the Airport 77

Before Mr. Zhang's Ford airplane arrived, the guards at Hongqiao Airport were ordered to deploy sentries around the perimeter of the field to prevent unauthorized personnel from entering. At the same time, Director of the Municipal Security Bureau Yang Hu also led a large detachment of armed security forces to the scene to provide adequate protection. Director of the Public Security Bureau Wen Hongen ordered the police in the relevant area to increase the number of police officers on duty, guarding both inside and outside the airport and at key intersections along the roads.

[Photograph of Zhang Xueliang arriving in Shanghai (photographed by Li Zunyong)]

Arrival and Landing Details 78

After the Ford airplane carrying Mr. Zhang and his party departed from Beiping in the morning, various dignitaries in Shanghai arrived at the airport one after another around 12:30 PM to welcome them, according to the expected itinerary. However, after waiting for three hours, the airplane had not yet arrived in Shanghai. Subsequently, Mr. Song Ziwen ordered the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Finance to inquire by radio. Around 3:00 PM, the airplane was spotted in the northeast corner of the airport. Soon, it flew closer and closer, and at 3:10 PM, it circled to the south and landed. After the airplane stopped, the Public Security Bureau's military band played music to welcome them. Mr. Zhang immediately exited the airplane amidst the music and shook hands with Wu Tiecheng, Song Ziwen, and others, exchanging a few words of greeting. After taking a group photo, he, along with his secretary Li Yingchao, advisor Donald, and Song Ziwen, rode in Song's car number "844" to the Song residence on Qizhi Road in the French Concession for a rest.

Mr. Zhang Appears Thin and Haggard 79

Those who arrived with Zhang Xueliang on the airplane yesterday included his secretary Li Yingchao, Western advisor Donald, three adjutants named Liu Wangyu, and medical officer Chen, as well as attendants, totaling nine people. Mr. Zhang wore a gray wool gabardine black sheepskin robe and Zhigong cloth shoes, appearing thin and haggard, but his spirits seemed quite high. His luggage was also very simple.

He Took a Nap at the Song Residence 80

After Mr. Zhang arrived at the Song residence, those who welcomed him also followed to the Song residence and sat and talked for half an hour. At that time, Mr. Zhang and those who welcomed him had not yet had lunch, so the Song residence prepared a meal for them. Later, because Mr. Zhang was tired from the journey, he took a nap at the Song residence. Those who welcomed him then took their leave separately. At 1:45 PM, he was accompanied by Acting President of the Executive Yuan Song to take a car to No. 181 Fuxu Road where he was staying. Mr. Zhang's residence at No. 181 Fuxu Road was temporarily rented by Du Yuesheng, and the President of the Executive Yuan Song dispatched six guards to take care of him. At the same time, the French Concession police and the Shanghai Municipal Council of the Public Concession also temporarily dispatched several detectives to guard the area, so the protection was very thorough. Because Fuxu Road is located at the border between the two concessions, it was decided for convenience to change the gate on Fuxu Road to the front gate on Julai Road for entry and exit.

Mayor to Host a Banquet This Afternoon 81

After Mr. Zhang arrived in Shanghai, Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Du Yuesheng, Yang Hu, and others all intended to host a banquet to welcome Mr. Zhang. At noon today, Mayor Wu Tiecheng will be the first to host Mr. Zhang. The location has been set at the Hong Kong Road Bank Club. Regarding Mr. Zhang's trip abroad, when reporters met Mayor Wu and others at the airport yesterday, they asked whether Zhang Hanqing would have to go abroad immediately after arriving in Shanghai. He said that Mr. Zhang arrived in Shanghai because he has been busy recently and also needs to complete passport procedures before going abroad, so he will have to stay in Shanghai for at least two weeks or so.

He Will Meet with Reporters Today 82

Yesterday, when Mr. Zhang arrived in Shanghai, reporters from various newspapers requested to speak with Mr. Zhang in person. Subsequently, Acting President of the Executive Yuan Song Ziwen informed the reporters that because Mr. Zhang was tired from the journey, he could not meet with them today (the 12th). Therefore, it was decided to invite reporters from various newspapers to the Ministry of Finance office at No. 501 West Ainsworth Road at 3:00 PM tomorrow.

He Released a Written Statement 83

Mr. Zhang released an extremely simple written statement last night, saying, "I have telegraphed my resignation in Beiping, sincerely informing all compatriots across the country that the Northeast Army is the army of the nation. As a soldier, I have already resigned from my post and returned the national army under my command to the central government. I no longer have any opinions that can be stated. As for me personally, I have been relieved of this heavy responsibility and can now spend my leisure time studying and cultivating myself, increasing my knowledge, and becoming a good citizen. This is something I have always sought but could not obtain. Now that I can achieve this hope, I deeply hope that members of society and my friends will all treat me as an ordinary citizen. How fortunate I am! As for national affairs, what I know is also what you know, so there is nothing I can tell you." Zhang Xueliang, 12th.

Municipal Party Headquarters Holds Eighth Anniversary Memorial of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Death 84

Chairman Jiang Huaisu Delivers a Somber Speech

Yesterday was the eighth anniversary of the death of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the leader of the Kuomintang. The municipal party headquarters convened various sectors to hold a memorial meeting at 9:00 AM in the auditorium of the party headquarters on Lin Yin Road. The details are recorded as follows:

Representatives Present 85

In addition to all the staff of the municipal party headquarters, representatives from various sectors who attended included Zhang Mengling from the Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Gao Jie and Li Wanqing from the Gao San Branch of the Court, Xu Qi from the Navigation Administration Bureau, Guan Zhijiang and Zheng Qingzhen from the First Special District Court, Zheng Letian from the Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Liu Binglin from the Jianghai Customs Supervisory Office, Li Yongxiang from the General Labor Union, representatives from the lighterage, cosmetics, cement, hat making, cotton spinning, military uniform, shipping, timber, and rubber industries labor unions, and representatives from Aiguo, Wuben, Junyi, Wanzhu, Peiben, Bide, Yihang, He'an, Yugong, Dongshan, Yangzheng, Dongming, Yongxing, and other schools, totaling over two hundred people. Chairman Jiang Huaisu presided, and Fan Mingyao served as master of ceremonies.

Memorial Ceremony 86

The memorial ceremony was as follows: (1) Opening, (2) Singing the party song, (3) Paying the highest respects to the party flag, the national flag, and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, (4) Chairman respectfully reading Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will, (5) Three minutes of silence, (6) Chairman's report, (7) Speech, (8) Shouting slogans, (9) Conclusion of the ceremony.

Chairman's Speech 87

After the ceremony, Chairman Jiang Huaisu gave a report, stating briefly that the people have lost their support since Dr. Sun Yat-sen left us eight years ago. The words and deeds of Dr. Sun Yat-sen during his lifetime are worthy of our permanent commemoration. Although Dr. Sun Yat-sen has been dead for eight years, the spirit of Dr. Sun Yat-sen has not died. Not only has it not died, but it is becoming brighter and brighter and becoming more evident with time. Now, in this time of serious national crisis, we should take the fearless spirit of Dr. Sun Yat-sen as our teacher in commemorating Dr. Sun Yat-sen. In the three minutes of silence, everyone's minds were thinking about the spirit of hard struggle of Mr. Sun Yat-sen during his lifetime. In the late Qing Dynasty, the national situation was more critical than it is now. If there had been no Dr. Sun Yat-sen to lead the revolution, China would have been divided up and jointly governed long ago. How could it have been maintained until today? Today, the people have a national concept in mind, but at that time, they only knew about their families and had no national thought. Now, if we want to save China from danger, we should implement Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will. When the September 18th Incident occurred, two provinces were lost. However, the people of Shanghai thought it was not in front of them and continued to enjoy themselves. It is truly a case of "the merchant girls do not know the hatred of a lost nation and still sing backyard flowers across the river." By the time of the January 28th Incident, the people of Shanghai were full of enthusiasm because the sound of gunfire was close. But now, if someone tells them about the situation in the Northeast, they don't care because there is no gunfire. It's really like "not burning incense in ordinary times, but hugging the Buddha's feet when things get urgent." But Shanghai was under airplane bombs last year, and the Northeast is now. The Party and the country are working hard to save the country by air, and they support and believe in the government to take unified steps. Next, He Wenbo from the Singapore Tongde News Agency gave a speech and then the meeting adjourned.

Memorial Slogans 88

(1) Commemorate Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the great personality, (2) Continue Dr. Sun Yat-sen's revolutionary spirit, (3) Complete Dr. Sun Yat-sen's revolutionary cause, (4) Commemorating Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death, we should have faith in doctrine and follow his last wishes, (5) Commemorating Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death, we must implement Dr. Sun Yat-sen's afforestation plan, (6) Commemorating Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death, we must work hard on political tutelage and construction,

(7) Strengthen the Party's unity and improve the Party's organization, (8) Prepare for armed resistance against Japanese aggression, (9) Compatriots across the country should reduce food consumption and donate enthusiastically to resist Japanese bandits, (10) Vow to recover the lost territory in the Northeast and wash away national shame, (11) Dr. Sun Yat-sen's spirit never dies, (12) Long live the Three Principles of the People!

Tree Planting Ceremony Held in the City and County Yesterday 89

Held separately in Donggou and Beiqiao Dachang

The fifth tree planting ceremony in this city was held at 10:00 AM yesterday in the Donggou Municipal Garden. Mayor Wu Tiecheng presided over the event. The details are recorded as follows:

The main entrance of the garden was decorated with pine and colored silk, with a plaque reading "Tree Planting Commemoration" hanging high. On both sides were couplets that said "Cultivating luxuriant forests is an elegant interest of the past sages" and "Promoting tree planting is a good garden of this world." The entrance to the tree planting area had couplets on both sides that said "Forests are brilliant, and all kinds of flowers are competing for glory" and "Gardens are quiet and secluded, and all kinds of flowers are competing for bloom." slogans were posted on the east and west sides. The Public Security Bureau dispatched the second company commander of the police, Yuan Guotang, and his team to maintain order.

Representatives Present 91

Those from various sectors who participated in the tree planting ceremony were transported from the Bund on Nanjing Road to Donggou. Those who attended included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Director of the Bureau of Social Affairs Wu Xingya, Director of the Bureau of Public Utilities Xu Peihuang, Director of the Public Security Bureau You Hongen, Director of the Bureau of Finance Cai Zengji, Director of the Bureau of Public Works Shen Yi, Director of the Bureau of Health Li Tingan, Director of the Bureau of Land Jin Liren, and all staff members, Liu Yide from the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Zhang Tianfu from the Special District Local Court, and teachers and students from Zhuyin, Xicheng, Shidai, Xigou, Sanxiu, Tanzhen, He'an, Bide, Wanzhu, and other elementary schools and Wusong, Wuben, Yangjing, and other middle schools, totaling over a thousand people.

Opening Ceremony 92

At 11:00 AM, the opening ceremony was held. Mayor Wu Tiecheng presided over the event. The Public Security Bureau military band played music, and the audience paid the highest respects to the party flag, the national flag, and the portrait of Dr. Sun Yat-sen. After three minutes of silence to commemorate Dr. Sun Yat-sen, the tree planting song was sung. The chairman then delivered a speech, and representatives from various sectors gave speeches in succession. Tree planting then began, and the event ended at 1:00 PM.

Opening Speech 93

Mayor Wu delivered an opening speech saying, "Ladies and gentlemen, today is the eighth anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death. Sun Yat-sen can be said to have lived for the Chinese nation and died for the Chinese nation. We who have not died should continue his unfinished will and implement all of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will one by one to achieve the goal of saving the country. Don't just talk about it and not do it. True followers of Dr. Sun Yat-sen who implement the Three Principles of the People should strive to implement Dr. Sun Yat-sen's national salvation plan and the new national salvation plan of this city. Therefore, the government has designated the anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death as Tree Planting Day to promote the tree planting movement. We were born in southern China, and we haven't seen forests everywhere. The wood used in our houses is mostly foreign goods. The reason for our annual floods and droughts is the lack of forests. Our most forested area is the three northeastern provinces. The huge forests cover hundreds of miles. The timber used by the people in the Northeast is all taken locally and does not need to be purchased from foreign countries. Not only is it sufficient for local use, but it can also be supplied to the south. However, the three northeastern provinces have been occupied by the Japanese. The forests in the northwest cannot be developed and transported due to inconvenient transportation. My country purchases about 14 million yuan of timber from foreign countries every year. Forests are closely related to people's health and floods and droughts. The afforestation movement should be promoted by the people of the whole country to save the country by planting trees. Planting trees is also saving the country. Our 400 million people are too uncompetitive. The Japanese have few people but a strong country, and their nation is prosperous. Our country has a large land and abundant resources, but it is only useful if we can use it. We should develop resources everywhere and work hard on production, so that money will not flow out and the country can turn from weak to strong and national shame can be washed away. Doing things must have a beginning and an end. I hope everyone will work hard."

Pan and Wang Deliver Speeches 94

Next, Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Municipal Bureau of Education, delivered a speech, briefly saying that today is the anniversary of the eighth anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death. Mayor Wu has talked about the significance of tree planting. I have seen various slogans today, saying that tree planting can increase people's health. This is indeed true, because trees can regulate the air and make people feel happy. Now I will only talk about the "planting" character in tree planting. The so-called "straight wood" can become good timber, just like a person's standing. But to produce good timber, we must protect it after planting. People in the student age need to increase their knowledge to become talents for society. Therefore, tree planting and being a person are equally important. Planting more trees becomes a forest, and joining groups becomes a strong nation. Therefore, I hope that the teachers and students of various schools who participate today will be inspired by this. Next, Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, delivered a speech, briefly saying that trees are planted and wood becomes timber, and people are upright and become useful. Therefore, tree planting and cultivating talents are equally important. To make tree planting excellent, we only need to pay attention to protection, but the cultivation of talents requires both teacher education and self-study. Therefore, I hope that all of you who participate today will work harder to become great talents, so that you will be useful to the country. Otherwise, I am afraid that there will be someone who is not as good as a tree.

Tree Planting in Beiqiao 95

Yesterday was the anniversary of the eighth anniversary of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's death.

Tree Planting in Dachang 96

Yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM, Jin Qingzhang, County Magistrate of Baoshan, led personnel from various agencies and people from all walks of life, about 500 people, to hold a tree planting ceremony next to the Dachang bus station. After the ceremony, County Magistrate Jin delivered a speech, briefly saying, "Now that spring has arrived, everyone can get up and plant trees. There are about two benefits to planting trees. First, don't the things we directly benefit from made of wood? Such as the stools we sit on, the tables we lie on, and the houses that shelter us from the wind and rain, are all made of trees. Therefore, the use of trees is greater than anything else, so we want everyone to get up and plant trees. The second is indirect benefits. Isn't my country often flooded? Because there is a lack of wood in the area. The ground with many trees can hold a large amount of water, so even heavy rain will not cause a disaster. If trees are planted next to the river bank, the river bank will not collapse, and trees can avoid wind disasters. If there are forests, the wind will be blocked, and crops will not suffer a tragic fate. In addition, it increases fun, and the benefits are endless. Let's all get up and plant trees quickly." The tree planting ceremony then concluded and the meeting adjourned.

申新一廠發生重大糾紛 101

Major Dispute Erupts at Shenxin Mill No. 1

Misunderstanding During Inspection Leads to Shooting of Workers, Outraging the Entire Factory, Causing a Strike; Party Headquarters Intervenes to Temporarily Resolve the Issue

According to Dagongshe, a major dispute occurred at Shenxin Mill No. 1 in Zhoujiaqiao, western Shanghai. During the evening shift change at 6:00 PM the night before, a misunderstanding arose when security guards searched workers, leading to a shooting that injured several workers. This incident sparked outrage among the factory's more than 9,000 workers, who immediately went on strike, creating a major disruption. Yesterday afternoon, after intervention by officials from the Municipal Party Headquarters and the General Labor Union, the situation was brought under control. Details of the incident are as follows:

肇事情形 102

Incident Details

According to the factory's practice, security guards hired by the factory inspect workers by name at the end of their shifts to prevent theft of yarn. The previous night, during the 6:00 PM shift change, a worker surnamed Wang and the head of the security guards, Li Nianfa, had a verbal altercation due to a misunderstanding. (On the 10th, a foreman named Liu Jinrong also had a dispute with security guards during an inspection, which was resolved after colleagues intervened.) As workers gathered during the shift change, the argument escalated, and violence broke out. Outnumbered, the security guards blew their whistles frantically. More than twenty security guards from across the factory rushed to the scene, leading to a major confrontation. Amid the chaos, security guards fired their weapons in an attempt to break free. Upon seeing the guards open fire, the workers fled in panic. More than ten workers fell into the Suzhou River while trying to cross the river by ferry, and more than twenty were injured in the crush. Eleven workers sustained serious gunshot wounds. Following the incident, the Zhoujiaqiao Police Station of the Sixth District Public Security Bureau dispatched a team of officers led by Inspector Wei to the scene to maintain order. Wen Hongen, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, and Tan, Director of the Sixth District, also arrived at the scene to inspect the situation after receiving reports.

全廠怠工 103

Factory-Wide Strike

Following the tragic incident, outrage spread among the factory's workers. More than 9,000 workers from the old and new factories spontaneously went on strike. They surrounded Deputy Factory Director Wang Yuncheng. Fan Shuquan and others, directors of the Tenth District Cotton Textile Workers' Union, arrived to mediate and prevent further escalation. The striking workers reported the incident to Party and government authorities and awaited a resolution.

工人傷勢 104

Worker Injuries

After the incident, the Tenth District Cotton Textile Workers' Union, together with factory representatives, sent the injured to the hospital for treatment. Yin Linquan was sent to the Red Cross Society with head and back injuries, with a bullet passing through his head. His condition is critical and life-threatening. Li Xiaohu suffered severe back injuries and remains in critical condition. Song Gendi was sent to Huilv Hospital with a gunshot wound to the leg, and the bullet has not yet been removed. Wang Xiaofa and Tan Gen suffered serious head injuries. Chen Boying and Yin Linquan were among three others who were treated for minor injuries and discharged from the hospital to return home. Police officers Zhu Yaozhong and Wu Guanshan, and security guards Xu Xingwu and Zhao Yongsou, also sustained minor injuries.

巡丁脱逃 105

Security Guards Flee

Witnesses at the scene identified Li Changfa, Wang Molin, and Gao Fengqi, the heads of the security guards, as the ones who fired the shots. Reports were made to the Sixth District Public Security Bureau, the factory, and the labor union to arrest them. However, when authorities dispatched officers to arrest them yesterday, the three had already fled.

黨政調處 106

Party and Government Mediation

The Tenth District Cotton Textile Workers' Union and representatives from the factory reported the incident to the Municipal Party Headquarters, the General Labor Union, and other organizations this morning, requesting assistance. The Municipal Party Headquarters dispatched Lu Yinchu, along with Li Yongxiang and Ye Xianggao from the General Labor Union, to the factory to mediate with worker representatives Zhuang Guanyong, Zhang Yilin, Yang Ada, and others, and factory director Yan Yukun. The following terms were agreed upon: (1) Starting immediately, all authority within the factory will be centralized under the control of Factory Director Yan; (2) The head of security guards will be dismissed and arrested for punishment; (3) The factory will provide medical expenses for the injured workers and advance condolence money to their families; (4) Wages will be paid as usual during the strike and recovery period; (5) Legal aspects are reserved. After Factory Director Yan accepted these terms, all workers expressed satisfaction. At 2:00 PM yesterday, workers resumed work under the guidance of representatives from the Municipal Party Headquarters and the General Labor Union, bringing the major dispute to a temporary end.

班禪代表昨抵滬 107

Panchen Lama's Representatives Arrive in Shanghai Yesterday

Anqin Hutuktu, along with a delegation of more than ten people, representatives dispatched by the Panchen Lama to Tibet to discuss reconciliation with the Dalai Lama, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing last night around 6:00 PM. They are scheduled to take a sea route to enter Tibet via India in the coming days.
