我國學術界紀念馬克司逝世五十週年 115

Chinese Academic Circles Commemorate the 50th Anniversary of Karl Marx's Death

This year, March 14th, marks the 50th anniversary of Karl Marx's death. Academic circles around the world are preparing for grand commemorations. It is reported that over a hundred people in Chinese academic circles, including Cai Yuanpei, Ye Yuhu, Jiang Hengyuan, Zhang Yunhe, Zhang Yi, Tao Zhixing, Li Gongpu, Zhu Duomin, Zhang Naiqi, Li Shishen, Chen Wangdao, and Huang Renzhi, are also initiating a memorial meeting for the 50th anniversary of Marx's death and are preparing to publish a commemorative volume of several hundred thousand words. The origin of the association is as follows: Karl Marx passed away on March 14, 1883. This year marks the 50th anniversary of his death. In these short fifty years, the impact of Marx's theories on the world has been significant. For fifty years, people around the world, whether they hated or loved, destroyed or praised Marx, have generally agreed that Marx was a great thinker and the founder of modern scientific socialism. In recent years, in our country, because of the opposition to the Communist Party, Marx's thoughts and theories have been implicated. Even those who speak of them are considered guilty, and those who study them are also considered guilty. This idea should be broken. The emergence of an idea and the establishment of a theory are not accidental miracles. If we can base ourselves on a pure academic research standpoint, then whether we agree or disagree, we should seriously study such ideas and theories. Only through research can we agree, and only through research can we disagree. Truth can only be approached through research. Now, because of the opposition to the Communist Party, Marx's thoughts and theories have been implicated. This is blind and is a kind of ideological Boxer Rebellion. We are now initiating the Memorial Meeting for the 50th Anniversary of Marx's Death based on a pure academic research standpoint, to pay sincere respect to this great modern thinker. At the same time, it is also a pioneering effort to promote freedom of research and freedom of thought and break the ideological Boxer Rebellion that has been prevalent in our country's academic circles in recent years. It is also reported that the Intellectual Development Department of the Shanghai YMCA on Eight Immortals Bridge will simultaneously hold a lecture series on scientific socialism, giving public lectures on the 14th and 15th of this month, from 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM each evening. The speakers have been confirmed as Cai Yuanpei, Zhang Naiqi, Li Shicen, and Chen Wangdao.

上海土布商店開幕紀 116

Record of the Opening of the Shanghai Native Cloth Store

The Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center, recognizing the growing crisis in the rural economy and the increasing encroachment of the Japanese, has been working to promote the cause of locally made cloths, focusing on production projects and the promotion of physical exercise. Last year, the center held two native cloth exhibitions that were well-received by people from all walks of life. To facilitate the need for cloth, the center initiated the establishment of the Shanghai Native Cloth Store at the Penglai Market on Penglai Road. At the time, a preparatory committee was organized, with Zhang Yi, Shi Yangyong, Zheng Yi, Ping Guanqiu, Shen Zhupo, Hu Wuxu, Wang Renfu, Peng Liren, Tang Shuming, Lu Jiren, and others jointly preparing for the store's opening. Prominent figures in the Party and state, as well as local gentry, have all expressed strong support. Preparations have been underway for three years, and the internal organization has been completed. Yesterday was the official opening day of the store, and visitors came in a constant stream. The details are recorded as follows:

到會代表 117

Representatives in Attendance

Shi She, Bi Huan, Lu Shixin, Sun Jichu, Sun Luo Hui, Li Shilin, He Degui, Ma Xingchou, Zhan Jiaji, Ye Chenghuai, Yang Mingqi, Sheng Jishan, Zhuo Kaijie, Zhang Fei, Zhang Yongnai, Zhang Bingquan, Wang Dingxian, Zhang Jin, Peng Liren, Yuan Xicheng, Hu Wuguang, Xu Guanghua, Huang Buyi, Xu Kexi, Shen Jinsong, Li Yunxing, Wang Yanqin.

開會情形 118

Meeting Proceedings

Chaired by Zhang Yi, Director of the Farmers' Education Center: (1) All stand at attention; (2) Pay the highest respect to the Party and national flags and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen; (3) The chairman recites Sun Yat-sen's will; (4) Silence; (5) Chairman delivers the opening speech; (6) Admonition; (7) Speeches; (8) Photograph; (9) The Municipal Citizens' Education Center Harmonica Band performs; (10) Tea and refreshments; (11) Ceremony concludes.

商店陳設 119

Store Display

The store's display is exquisite and impressive. All products are hand-woven by rural farmers, using entirely domestic raw materials. The patterns and colors are designed by the county's native cloth improvement program. Items such as overcoat fabric, old-patterned cloth, Yunxia cloth, Heping cloth, Ziyou cloth, Xuechi cloth, and Fendou cloth are most suitable for modern wear. To offer preferential treatment to patriotic individuals, the store offers uniform discounts on all cloth items. From 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM in the afternoon, the store offers old rescue cloth most suitable for the current era, selling each bolt for only one yuan and six cents.

主席致辭 120

Chairman's Speech

The chairman's opening speech stated that today is the opening ceremony of the Shanghai Native Cloth Store, and it is an honor to have everyone present. The establishment of the Shanghai Native Cloth Store is intended to promote the sale of authentic domestic native cloth and to increase farmers' production. Shanghai is a large metropolis with a vast territory and a large population, so it is necessary to start with Shanghai to promote sales, which will be more effective. Farmers in this county engage in weaving as a sideline in addition to farming. In recent years, foreign goods have flooded the market, and the proportion of Chinese people wearing native cloth is less than two-tenths, resulting in sluggish sales of native cloth and a deteriorating livelihood for farmers. Our country is based on agriculture, and if the rural economy collapses, then the vitality of the nation will inevitably decline. Our country has a population of 400 million. If everyone buys 3 yuan less of foreign goods each year, then we can reduce the outflow of money by 1.2 billion yuan each year. This is of great significance to the national economy. I hope everyone will pay attention to it. In recent years, the dumping of Japanese cotton fabrics into China has been astonishing, and unscrupulous merchants are recklessly passing off inferior goods as domestic goods to deceive the Chinese people, which is extremely distressing. Now, the Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center and others, in light of the above, are working hard to improve native cloth, and the quality of the products has been improving in recent years, comparable to imported goods. Moreover, the government is also working hard to promote it, and both the business tax and export tax on native cloth are exempt. The purpose is to (1) defeat the economic aggression of the imperialists, (2) relieve the bankruptcy of the rural economy. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Municipal Education Bureau are visiting all sectors and schools to promote native cloth as much as possible. Therefore, I hope that everyone present today will work hard to spread the word, which will be fortunate for the country.

局長訓辭 121

Director's Admonition

Shi She, Director of the County Education Bureau, gave an admonition, stating that the poor state of China's economy has reached an extreme point. Most of the reason for this is that the Chinese people do not like to use domestic goods. In the past few years, the bankruptcy of the national economy has become worse and worse, and the suffering of farmers is particularly deep. Now, the Shanghai Farmers' Education Center has established the Native Cloth Store in order to alleviate this crisis, which can prevent the outflow of profits and increase farmers' production. Therefore, I hope that all sectors will make every effort to promote it. Zhang Shi, Peng Liren, Xu Guanghua, Bi Huan, and others then gave speeches. (Speeches omitted for length.)

股東會議 122

Shareholders Meeting

The store held a shareholders meeting yesterday afternoon, attended by Lu Jiren, Zhang Yi, Chen Linfu, Luo Bingchu, Sun Zhangchuan, Chen Aikang, Kuang Zhongmou, Zhang Yingxiang, Chen Shuding, Wang Renfu, Ji Baoyu, Ping Guanqiu, and others. Chaired by Zhang Yi, after performing the formalities, he reported on the purpose of establishing the store, the organization process, and future wishes, followed by discussions: (1) Approved the store's charter; (2) Appointed Shen Zhupo, Tang Shuming, and Hu Wu as supervisors, Kuang Rongyu as alternate supervisor, and Zhang Yingxiang as manager; (3) Confirmed that the store's main business would be native cloth, with various domestic goods as a supplementary business. 海關佈告禁止運雜糧往東北 123

Therefore, it is necessary to comply with the order. Merchants are hereby notified.

川軍勦赤捷電 124

Sichuan Army Victory Telegram in Suppressing the Communists

Wang Ya'te, the representative of the Sichuan-Shaanxi Border Area Communist Suppression Supervisory Office stationed in Shanghai, received a telegram from Tian Songyao, which stated: "To Wang Shuxian in Shanghai, according to the report from Commander-in-Chief Sun Zhen, our army's Central Column, Luo Naiqiong's division, and a part of the Right Column, Zeng Xiandong's division, after a fierce battle this morning at 9:00 AM, captured Bazhong City. The communist bandits suffered heavy casualties and are retreating in disarray. We are currently pursuing them, etc."

Another telegram stated: "Urgent, to Wang Shuxian in Shanghai, (1) Commander Luo's column has not yet telegraphed that our Zhu and Song regiments completely occupied Bazhong City at 9:00 AM this morning. The bandits retreated towards Jianshanping, Qingjiangdu, and Silinchang. Our army is currently pursuing them from Wangwang Mountain, Chaqi Mountain, and Tazi Mountain. (2) Division Commander Liu's telegram stated that the Yang Xiulv regiment has dispatched teams to pursue the bandits from the front of Luojiaba and has now pursued them to the vicinity of Daheitan. This morning, the Hu Jie and Zhang Xiaokang regiments were also dispatched to attack the bandits in the Dayuhui Yinmuba Wulangmiao area. (3) Commander of the Fifth Column reported that the Tong regiment, which was attacking Zhugezhai, has suffered many casualties after repeated attacks. Although mortars were used for bombing, it was not successful. Therefore, in the evening, company commander Zhang Renjie led troops at night, using human ladders to climb over the rocks and enter the fortress. At the same time, platoon leader Li Mingnian and warrant officer He Zhonglin led plainclothes teams to feign attacks from the front. By midnight, our night raiding troops had completely entered the fortress, and the plainclothes teams took the opportunity to swarm in. Therefore, although there were over a thousand bandits, they were all at a loss and fled, falling off the rocks. In this battle, over 300 bandits were killed, including two company commanders, and over a hundred firearms and countless supplies were seized. Our army also suffered 80 to 90 casualties among officers and soldiers. (4) Commander He's telegram stated that Guling Bamiya was first occupied by Lü's regiment of the First Division at dawn. The bandits had no way to retreat and fled in disarray, except for a portion that had previously fled to Zhaizi Xindianzi. Xie Anhua's regiment pursued them to Luojiaba, and the units were blocking and killing the fleeing bandits, which was extremely fierce. Therefore, many bandits fell off the rocks and into the water, and many were captured alive. Even more firearms and supplies were abandoned. (5) Overseer Liu's telegram stated that the Red Army's Tenth Division launched a fierce attack on our Qinglongzhai this morning. Liao's column commander dispatched Wang's regiment to raid the bandits' left flank in Changlezhai and Chen's regiment to raid the bandits' right flank. After a fierce battle until dusk, the officers and soldiers on the fortress rushed down and threw bombs, killing over 200 bandits, and the bandit's fortifications were abandoned. (6) Commander Luo's telegram stated that according to the confession of a surrendered bandit carrying a gun, the elite troops of the bandits were severely damaged in the Changchi battle, resulting in a disastrous defeat. As a result, many bandit officers were dismissed, placed under surveillance, and executed. Recently, the bandits have been divided into several factions, with some advocating defending to the death and others advocating abandoning Tongnanba. There is a great tendency to split up, etc."

Two Charity Organizations Assist the Shaanxi Disaster 125

Chinese and Foreign Relief Society: The Chinese and Foreign Relief Society at 12 Renji Road highly values the disaster situation in Shaanxi Province and is sparing no effort in providing relief. According to recent news from the province, last year's wheat harvest in the northwest was almost completely lost. Although there were some soybeans after July, they were insufficient to alleviate the situation. Houses and livestock were sold everywhere, and even fertile land was offered at two yuan per acre, but no one was willing to buy. Residents have fled en masse. Currently, only a few porridge kitchens are maintaining the lives of orphaned children. Upon learning of this tragic situation, the society resolved to purchase a large quantity of relief rice and transport it to Shaanxi for distribution, and to establish multiple porridge kitchens in the disaster areas, costing approximately two thousand yuan per month. Recently, they specially dispatched staff member Mr. Zheng Nansheng to Pukou and other places to purchase miscellaneous sugar, and the Ministry of Railways agreed to provide free transportation to Shaanxi. The first batch of three thousand five hundred and seventy bags has already been loaded by the Jinpu Railway Bureau and directly transported to Tongguan. The second batch of one thousand one hundred and thirty bags will also be shipped out within days. The value of the relief rice is over forty thousand yuan, of which over one thousand five hundred bags were purchased by the Jisheng Society for joint transportation to assist Wugong and other areas in Shaanxi. The Shaanxi disaster has been ongoing for years, and the disaster area is vast. Although there is this large quantity of relief rice, it is like a drop in the bucket and is unlikely to provide substantial relief. It is hoped that charitable individuals both at home and abroad will act with compassion and contribute generously. It must be understood that in these times of national crisis, saving others is saving oneself. Each person saved adds a bit to the country's strength to resist aggression. This not only accumulates merit but also benefits the nation.

Jisheng Society: The Chinese Jisheng Society of this city considers the disaster situation in Shaanxi Province to be particularly severe. The society has previously allocated five thousand yuan to the Jisheng Branch in the province for porridge kitchen expenses and five thousand yuan to the Wugong County shelter, and is currently carrying out relief efforts. Now, as the disaster situation in Wugong, Fufeng, and other counties in the province continues to worsen and grain prices soar, even the middle class are lamenting their empty homes, let alone the poor disaster victims. The Chinese and Foreign Relief Society is shipping two thousand shi of rice to Shaanxi, selecting those most in need for distribution. The society is also transporting one thousand seven hundred shi of relief rice for shipment to Shaanxi to save dying disaster victims. This is only a small portion of the granary. At this time of popular poverty, how can everyone embrace patriotism and make compassionate vows, so that both the northeast and northwest disaster situations can benefit from their generosity? Looking forward, we cannot help but reverently pray.

Work of the Shanghai Municipal Council Public Works Department Last Year 126

The Commissioner of Public Works of the Shanghai Municipal Council, Mr. Hapgood, stated in his work report for 1932 that the work of the year was unable to maintain normalcy due to the impact of the Sino-Japanese conflict at the beginning of the year, especially in the northern and eastern districts. In February and part of March, the normal public works of these two districts were completely suspended. Most of the staff of the department were used to prepare barbed wire and other fortifications, and vehicles were also concentrated for military emergencies.

Private Construction: Due to the war and other factors, the total value of private construction permits issued this year was only over 18 million taels, only half of that of 1931 (which was over 37 million taels, and 1930 was over 46 million taels). A total of 1,190 applications were received, and 1,218 were approved. The number of old houses demolished was 2,054 Chinese-style and 78 Western-style, most of which were demolished and rebuilt. The staff of the Public Works Department were insufficient to handle the supervision of building regulations. A total of 1,063 violations were discovered and notified during the year, and there were 821 cases of work being carried out without permits. Also, the demolition of old houses, such as the theater at the corner of Er Ma Road and Zhejiang Road, the theater on San Ma Road, and five Chinese-style houses on Edward Road, all experienced accidents, mostly due to the lack of sufficient supervision by specialized personnel.

Elimination of Sheds: The many shacks of the poor in the concession have long been a problem. In 1931, a registration was conducted to facilitate elimination. A total of 2,041 numbers were registered. At the beginning of this year, due to the situation, surveillance was slightly relaxed, and many more were built. It was then resolved to issue a one-month notice to demolish them. A total of 550 were demolished in October. It is very difficult to effectively manage this matter, but this year's method may serve as a warning.

Garbage Removal: This year, 285,776 tons of household garbage were removed, 29,923 tons of street sweepings, and 23,152 tons of sewage from ditches, averaging 928 tons per day. A small portion was transported by boat, and the remainder was used to fill low-lying areas. 38,502 tons were sent to the incinerators on Binlang Road and Maohai Road for incineration. At the end of the year, the furnace on Binlang Road incinerated about 163 tons per day, and the furnace on Maohai Road incinerated about 23 tons per day. The contractor for transporting garbage performed satisfactorily this year, so they have been approved to continue for another year. From mid-March to mid-June, Public Works employees cleared 7,577 tons of garbage in the area north of the concession.

Road Construction: There were no major projects in road construction this year. Roads widened include Avenue Road, Race Course Road, Fuzhou Road, North Sichuan Road, etc., totaling 229,970 square yards of road surface and subgrade. The total length of roads converted to cement-mixed subgrade and paved with asphalt was 1.736 miles. In short, road construction has been delayed for too long, and the accumulation of large-scale projects will become increasingly heavy.

Drainage Works: A total of 1.358 miles of drainage ditches were laid, with pipe diameters ranging from 6 inches to 4 feet 6 inches. Branch pipes were laid for a length of 2.815 miles. Sewage ditches were completed for 4.535 miles, with diameters ranging from 6 inches to 18 inches. Branch pipes were laid for a length of 0.305 miles. Due to unpaid fees, the contractor for cleaning sewage has been replaced.

Land Acquisition: To widen and extend roads, 47 mu, 9 fen, and 4 li of land were acquired this year, involving 121 transactions, with a total payment of 1,413,538 taels. In addition, 11 mu, 5 fen, 5 li, and 9 hao of land were acquired for the expansion of parks and cemeteries, with a payment of 147,413 taels. The land prices were sent to the Land Committee for evaluation four times, and the evaluated price was approximately 47% lower than the original asking price. In addition, the Shanghai Municipal Council also sold several parcels of land, the most important of which was 1.799 mu at the corner of Fuzhou Road and Jiangxi Road, which fetched 371,494 taels, and 2.943 mu at the corner of Chengdu Road and Jing'an Temple Road, which fetched 331,220 taels.

Public Buildings: The various public buildings of the Shanghai Municipal Council that were built and completed this year include the police station on Chengdu Road, Grant Road, and Yulin Road, the police dormitory on Carter Road and Baoding Road, the police hospital on Ward Road, the expansion of the prison on Ward Road, including offices, cells, juvenile cells, workshops, laundry, inmate hospital, and guard residences, the slaughterhouse on Sazelu Road, the Victoria Hospital on Daxi Road, the sanitation branch on Xiaoshadu Road, the small vegetable market on Shankaigong Road, Xiaoshadu Road, and Bianqu Road, the incinerators on Binlang Road and Maohai Road, and the Chinese children's schools on Xinwen Road and Jingzhou Road, etc. In addition, there are the Tangen Road Bridge, the Hongkou Creek bank, and the wharves on Chefoo Road and Chaofeng Road.

Page 11

The Kidnapping of Korean Mr. Li Chunshan 127

A Long and Tragic Tale, A Major Loss for the Korean Revolution

Since the kidnapping of Korean revolutionary leader Li Chunshan on Luban Road in the Chinese area of ​​Nanshi a few days ago (the 9th), it has aroused deep concern and great attention from Chinese and foreign people in this city. Yesterday, a reporter from this newspaper specially interviewed a certain important Korean personage, a close friend of Mr. Li, to inquire about his views on this case. He was immediately informed one by one, and he recounted in detail Mr. Li's personal experiences and his history of struggle (the following are the words of the gentleman):

Young and Ambitious 128

Mr. Li is a native of Hongxi-dong, Yizhou-myeon, Yizhou-gun, Pyeonganbuk-do, Korea, and is now forty-nine years old. He lost his father at an early age and was raised by his virtuous widow mother. He was young and ambitious. He initially graduated from Boseong Law School in Gyeongseong, and lamented the fall of his motherland. At the age of twenty-two, he joined the New People's Association and devoted himself to the mass movement. He was arrested once and exiled to a deserted island for a year. After returning to the country, his ambition grew stronger, and he continued to work hard in the revolutionary movement.

Revolutionary Work 129

In 1919, when the Korean Independence Movement was at its peak, Li came to Shanghai to assist Mr. An Chang-ho, who is now trapped, in organizing the Provisional Government. At that time, An served as the Acting President and Prime Minister, and Li served as the Secretary-General. Later, the committee system was changed, and Li served as the Minister of the Interior. Recently, he was appointed as the Director of Political Affairs of the Korean Residents Association. When Mr. Li's work was the most intense, he organized the Restoration Society and the Labor Soldiers Association, and published publications such as the "Blood History of the Korean Independence Movement."

Chinese Nationality 130

According to Mr. Li's original name, Chun-gap, he became a Chinese citizen at the age of thirty-six (1920) and held a naturalization certificate. Last year, the certificate was suddenly lost. He received the No. 11 Nationality Certificate issued by the Ministry of the Interior of the National Government on January 19 of this year. Li's family lives at No. 54 Baokang Lane, Avenue Joffre, French Concession, but since the end of the January 28th Shanghai Incident and the bombing case in Hongkou Park, Li has been in a very dangerous situation.

Fratricide 131

Mr. Li's situation is actually not dangerous overnight. Does the reporter still remember that last year, at No. 13 Luban Road, French Concession, a detective from a certain country used kidnapping to forcibly kidnap a Korean citizen? At that time, it was actually a trap set by a certain country to capture Li. If you are not annoyed, I would like to trace back and tell you. According to Mr. Li's generous nature, he loves to socialize. If there is a request for a fallen Korean, he can especially help him out. This is your chivalrous nature. I did not expect that the same kind would plan to kill each other.

Designed to Trap 132

One evening, a Korean came to Li's house to visit Li, stating that he had been unemployed for a long time and lacked the means to make a living. He planned to set up a small cafe with friends at No. 13 Luban Road, and asked Li to help him with funds to make it happen. Li readily agreed. Unexpectedly, this Korean was bribed by a detective from a certain country and specially set up this plan to kidnap Li. When the time came, the Korean insisted that Li go to No. 13 to discuss everything with the landlord. Li went with him. After sitting in the room for a while, the Korean suddenly left the room on the pretext.

Escaped Once 133

At that time, there was still a Korean in the room. Knowing that a great disaster was coming to Mr. Li, he realized his conscience and took advantage of the Korean's departure to give Li instructions. Li awoke and fled through the front door. However, as soon as he left the alley, a detective from a certain country had already tracked him into the room. When he chased after Li, it was too late, so he arrested the Korean who had given Li instructions. At that time, after Li escaped, he came to me and told me. I kept him for dinner and filled him with a glass of fine wine to celebrate his escape.

Detective Followed 134

Since then, Li has been living in seclusion in the Chinese area of ​​Nanshi, and I have also moved to Luban Road with most of the Koreans to ensure safety. Unexpectedly, since we moved to the Chinese area, a large number of plainclothes detectives from a certain country have been constantly found near the bridge connecting the Chinese and French areas (ie, the junction of Luban Road and Luban Road), secretly monitoring our actions. However, although these people are disguised in Chinese clothes, various characteristics such as the habitual way of walking in wooden clogs, as well as their figure and skin, cannot escape the eyes of our Koreans.

Trying to Rescue 135

Now, Mr. Li has become a bird in a cage, meat on a chopping board. This is not only Mr. Li's misfortune, but also Korea's misfortune. All the Korean citizens are now actively trying to rescue him, but the facts of the case are obvious. Mr. Li is a poor revolutionary and cannot be compared to an ordinary kidnapping for ransom. Moreover, people from a certain country have had a precedent for kidnapping Korean citizens in the French Concession, so the content of this case is self-evident. At this time, what all Korean citizens hope is how your country's Chinese authorities can find a way to rescue him.

Better Late Than Never 136

What I find most alarming is that when the Korean citizens moved into the Chinese area, they repeatedly requested the competent Second District General Administration to pay more attention to protection, but for almost a year, there has been almost no post on Luban Road. When Mr. Li was kidnapped, he shouted for help, and more than ten passers-by gathered. If there were police officers on duty nearby, Mr. Li might have been spared, or at least the license plate number of the car could have been copied for investigation. However, things have come to this, what else can be said? But after the incident, District Chief Jin of the Second District temporarily added a post in Likou to protect us. The people of the subjugated country have received this great gift, and we are already deeply grateful. We cannot say that it is locking the door after the thief has left, we can only say that it is better late than never. When he said this, he sighed incessantly, and the reporter could only smile bitterly and retreat.

French Fugitive Arrested on German Ship 137

The Fugitive Military Criminal, Schwalbe

The North China Daily News reported that the French fugitive military criminal Schwalbe, who had been extensively searched for six months by French police and detectives in the ocean below the equator, was arrested again on the German merchant ship Kumoran in Shanghai yesterday evening (11th). Schwalbe was stationed in the Far East with the Urmi Michel military ship in 1927. Because he attempted to kill an officer, he was sentenced to death, which was later reduced to life imprisonment and sent to French Guiana in South America for service. The place is directly north of the equator, and the rocks are melting all year round. Schwalbe served for six years and could not bear the pain, so he and three military criminals drove a small boat, carrying fresh water and food, and stole away at night. They were not caught by the chasing ship or overturned by the wind and waves, and arrived at Trinidad, 800 miles away. He then found a job on a German ship, which sailed to Hamburg. After arriving in Germany, he was unemployed for a while, and then joined the Norddeutscher Lloyd's Kumoran ship and came to Shanghai. Detectives in the French Concession of this city had previously received a report that the ship arrived in Shanghai yesterday, and identified Schwalbe as working as a cook on the ship. They immediately notified the French police station, and detectives from the French detective agency and the Tilanqiao police station boarded the ship last night and arrested him.

Chen Er'a Is Extremely Shameless 146

He Not Only Abducts and Elopes With Someone Else's Daughter but Also Conspires to Commit Assault

Chen Hongsheng, a 54-year-old local man, makes a living by farming. His home is at No. 25 Longhua Road, Southwest Township. Chen has a daughter named Jinbao, who is 19 years old and waiting to be married. There was a Zhang Er'a from Suzhou, who was 21 years old. In the 20th year of the Republic of China, Zhang worked as a handyman in a shipyard in Longhua. Therefore, in order to facilitate his travel back and forth, he lived near Chen's house with several colleagues. He usually went in and out and saw Jinbao. Although she was a farmer's daughter, she was beautiful and slender. He could not help but be moved, so he took advantage of his free time to tempt her with romantic words and try to seduce her. At that time, Jinbao's love affair was just beginning, and she was fascinated by him. Soon, they became entangled and had a physical relationship. However, because she was embarrassed in front of Chen, she could not do what she wanted, so they agreed to take away Chen's savings of 80 silver dollars, two gold rings, and a pair of gold earrings and elope to the countryside of Suzhou, where they lived together in Zhang's home, intending to live happily ever after. However, Zhang was originally a thief, and after returning to his hometown, he lacked work and had no income, so the family's livelihood became increasingly difficult, and his temperament also changed greatly. He was no longer as gentle and considerate to Jinbao as he was at the beginning. He would often beat her if she disobeyed him slightly, but Jinbao eventually tolerated it. Unexpectedly, Zhang recently ran out of money and suddenly had evil thoughts. He planned to sell Jinbao for money, but the plan was not secret and was discovered by Jinbao. She was greatly shocked and took advantage of Zhang's unpreparedness on January 12 of this year to sneak into Shen and return to her home. She told her father the truth and deeply regretted it. Chen scolded her severely and then asked someone to introduce her to work as a female worker in the Longzhang Paper Mill, where she went out early and returned late every day, and did not let her go out during her free time in order to restrain her. Unexpectedly, Zhang was still unwilling after Jinbao left, so he tracked her to Shanghai and conspired with others to wait on the roadside near the paper mill at about 5:00 a.m. on the morning of the day. After a while, he saw Jinbao coming to work, so he rushed forward and forced her to return to Suzhou. The woman refused to the death. Zhang immediately twisted her to the ground, beat her severely, and used an iron rod to injure her head and legs, causing her to bleed profusely. The woman shouted for help. Zhang and others then dispersed. Before leaving, they said that tomorrow morning at 7:00, I will wait for you at a tea house on Lichang Bridge Street outside Xiaonanmen in Nanshi to have a cup of tea. If you don't come, be careful of your dog's life. When the woman saw Zhang and others go far away, she returned home and told her father. Chen was very angry after hearing this, so he went to the tea house on Guocang Bridge at about 7:00 a.m. yesterday with his relative Sun Changfu and others to reason with Zhang. The two sides disagreed and suddenly started a conflict. The guard police Li Jinming from the 13th post heard the news and rushed to the scene and took both sides into the jurisdiction of the Third Division of the First District. After a preliminary hearing by the director, Zhang was deemed to have abducted someone else's daughter and dared to conspire to commit assault, which was extremely hateful. He immediately ordered that a document be prepared and sent to the bureau for interrogation.

Socialite Xue Jinyuan Accused of Indecent Assault on Italian Boy 156

Glamorous nightlife is the door to seduction, secret chats are the path to pleasure. The Italian boy was infected with a venereal disease, so his father was outraged and sued Xue criminally.

Since the open prevalence of social interactions, and the breaking down of boundaries between men and women, matters that are detrimental to public morals are not only heard of every day, but also emerge in an endless stream. However, in the past, it was only men who seduced women, causing them to engage in immoral behavior. But recently, it has escalated, and there have been cases of women attempting to commit indecent acts and abducting men. What is particularly strange is that the man who was seduced was an uncrowned European boy. This is truly what is meant by the vastness of Shanghai, where there is nothing that is not strange. Although this matter has not yet been widely publicized in society, it has already been involved in litigation. Therefore, the family backgrounds of both parties and the original complaint are recorded as follows:

Family Backgrounds of Both Parties 157

The woman's name is Xue Jinyuan, a native of Lingnan. Her age has passed her prime, but she is still unmarried. Her father runs a business in Hong Kong, is skilled in business dealings, and has a reputation for being wealthy. Jinyuan went to school from a young age, so she is proficient in both Chinese and Western literature, and is particularly good at socializing. She had already earned the reputation of a socialite in various ports in Hong Kong and Macau. Later, she came to Shanghai and gained the title of a social star in society. Her sister, Jintuan, is the wife of a certain important figure in the aviation industry. Currently, Jinyuan resides at 111 Jiande Fang, Yuyuan Road, in western Shanghai. The man, on the other hand, is Italian, named Josepb, who is nineteen years old and studying at a Western-run university. His father is L.T.Jovino, who is currently the general manager of the Yishang Ning Shipping Company, and resides at 566 Disiwei Road, Hongkou.

Process of Association 158

Mr. You Weiwu is a navigator. Once, when he and his wife were living in Macau, Xue Jinyuan also happened to be traveling in Macau, and they were neighbors. Therefore, they got to know each other. Later, due to business reasons, Mr. You brought his family to Shanghai, and Miss Xue also came without prior arrangement. They were overjoyed to meet again. Jinyuan likes dancing, and every night she would invite Mr. You's son, Daishi Fu, to go to the dance hall, and would not return until they were tired. Mr. and Mrs. You initially thought that their son was still young and did not suspect that any impropriety would occur, so they did not prohibit it at all. However, Jinyuan had already identified this blond-haired, blue-eyed child as nothing less than a resurrected Song Yu or a reborn Pan An. After successfully seducing him, they actually lived together. The boy, who knew nothing, fell in love with Xue Jinyuan.

Love, and became more and more confused. Not only did he have no intention of studying, but he also felt uneasy when eating and sleeping. He had to find excuses to go out alone every day, either holding hands with Jinyuan for a walk, or riding in the same car. She originally had a 1707 Baden Austin car, and she could drive herself. Every time the moon was bright and the wind was clear, this pair of lovers would drive through the city and suburbs to enjoy themselves. One snowy night, their car was speeding along, passing Yangshupu in the eastern district. The woman was enjoying the scenery, and in her boundless joy, she wanted her lover to show off his driving skills. However, Yoshio Fu had never learned this skill, but he wanted to win the favor of his beauty, so he risked it. Who knew that he was inexperienced in driving, and a disaster occurred. A Japanese soldier happened to be passing by, and three soldiers were injured. The injured soldiers saw that the driver was an Italian, so they filed a complaint with the Italian Consulate in Shanghai. This case has not yet been concluded. Although You Weiwu had already heard that his son and Jinyuan were in the same car and injured people, he still did not know the whole story. Recently, because his son suddenly suffered from a certain hidden disease, he finally understood everything and was extremely angry. He immediately decided to hire lawyer Yang Ruinian to file a criminal complaint against Xue Jinyuan in the First Special District Court. At the same time, he strictly disciplined his son. However, Xue Jinyuan still did not know that she had been accused. On the 18th of this month, when Yoshio Fu reached the age of eighteen, she specially spent a lot of money to make a set of Western-style clothes and took them to him as a gift, expressing her intention to add to his life. Her affection can be said to be sincere.

The Original Complaint 159

For intending to commit indecent acts and abducting a young man and disrupting the family, I respectfully request your careful examination, prompt detention, and severe punishment according to the law, and reserve the right to private prosecution. I, the plaintiff, work in the shipping industry and have lived in China with my wife and son for twenty-one years. In the spring of that year, when I was living in Macau, the defendant, Xue Jinyuan, was also living there, so we got to know each other and began to associate with each other. Later, I brought my family to Shanghai, and the defendant also moved here. Old acquaintances in a new place, our association became closer. My eldest son, Yoshiou Fu, is not yet seventeen years old. Because of our close association, we became intimate with each other. Social interactions are open, which is the fashion of the times. The principle of not touching between men and women has long been a formality. The ancient country of the East does not even prohibit it, let alone I, the plaintiff, who am a European? Moreover, my eldest son is not yet an adult and is still an Italian citizen. The defendant is already past her prime, and the age difference is significant. I did not suspect anything else. If I were to prohibit their association, wouldn't it be too pedantic? Therefore, I, the plaintiff, did not prohibit it. Who knew that the defendant, a young woman, was careless and had no husband. She climbed over the wall to peep at Song Yu. At times, she would invite him to dance together, and at times, she would go in and out of theaters. I, the plaintiff, thought that singing, dancing, banquets, and outings were common human affairs. However, the defendant used glamorous nightlife as a door to seduction, and secret chats as a path to pleasure. She used the ups and downs of music to move his heartstrings, and the dazzling beauty to fan his flames of desire. How could I have expected this? The boy was ignorant and did not know how to love himself, so he was seduced and committed immoral acts. At first, he still had some scruples, and only returned late at night. Later, he became less and less afraid and dared to stay overnight for several nights. I, the plaintiff, could not forbid him and could not sever the relationship. As a result, Yoshio Fu became dazed and had no intention of studying, and was expelled from school. It is truly lamentable. Recently, Yoshio Fu was infected with a venereal disease, and his strong body has now become emaciated and is on the verge of death. The defendant's actions have not only harmed Yoshio Fu, but also damaged the happiness of the family. She is a scourge to society and a huge villain. Recently, on the 25th of last month, at 11:00 PM on a snowy night, she used her own car, driven by Yoshio Fu, to speed along the Yangshupu Road area. On a deserted suburban night, a man and a woman were in the same car. Such behavior can be used to guess her intentions. Again, she was careless and injured three Japanese soldiers. The injuries were very serious. The Japanese side is about to sue Yoshio Fu in the Italian Consulate. According to Italian civil law and the regulations of the Engineering Bureau, the responsibility for this damage should be borne by the car owner and the licensee. The car owner in this case is a citizen of the Republic of China and has no jurisdiction. Although the case has not yet been concluded, Yoshio Fu will inevitably have to bear the responsibility. I, the plaintiff, am Yoshio Fu's father, so I cannot escape the responsibility of compensating him. All of these losses were caused by the defendant's seduction, so the defendant should be responsible. Therefore, I request that the right to private prosecution be reserved and that the defendant be charged with indecent assault and abduction, which violates Article 257, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law. I respectfully request that your honorable court promptly summon her to maintain public morals and uphold the law.

The presiding judge has issued summonses and sent police to notify both the plaintiff and the defendant to appear in court on time to await interrogation. This romantic lawsuit involving the private affairs of men and women is sufficient to break the new record of all romantic cases in Shanghai over the years. It is expected that on the day of the trial, scoundrels, beauties, and other people will leave their homes and go to the courthouse to listen to the trial.

Reader Consultant

Marriage Issues 162

丨 Letter from Mr. Wang Muchong of Nanjing

I have a question to ask you! I hope you can provide guidance. The fact is this: My life grew up entirely within the feudal power of society, so my marriage was also completely involuntary and arranged by my parents through matchmakers. I remember when I was eight years old, my parents arranged my engagement to a Miss Li from the same village. At that time, I was still young, and of course, there was no talk of autonomy or freedom, resistance or opposition. I only knew how to read the Three Character Classic: "As a child, be filial to your parents," and knew nothing else. When I was studying in middle school, I wanted to express my disagreement with marrying an illiterate person, but because I was not economically independent and could not break away from family ties, arguing with my family would have meant immediately dropping out of school, so I could not get my wish. At the age of seventeen (in 1930), I graduated from a certain provincial middle school in Guizhou. At this time, my parents and elders of the clan were extremely happy to see me return from studying in the provincial capital (Guiyang), so they all came to urge my parents to set a date for my wedding. At this time, I was preparing to go abroad to study and repeatedly refused. However, the "me of the past" was not strong enough to break through that environment, so I temporarily succumbed. As for that Miss Li, she is the daughter of a wealthy man, uneducated and illiterate. My family was not very well-off, but her family was rich. I don't know why her parents insisted on marrying her to me. My parents' minds were just like hers! Feudal! Stubborn! I was extremely unwilling! First, she is illiterate. However, after being forced to marry her, I still continued to study, determined not to change my ambition. Our feelings for each other were ordinary, neither warm nor cold. Later, what I least expected was that she turned out to be a literate country girl. However, she is very gentle in nature and very humble and yielding to me, not arrogant, and she follows my decisions in everything. She is especially respectful to my parents. However, I am still just ordinary towards her because she is illiterate, does not understand human affairs, and does not know the trends of the world. She knows even less about the true meaning of the union of men and women and of marriage. A person like this is no different from a wooden puppet, and originally, it was not a voluntary union. In my opinion, her strengths cannot compensate for her weaknesses. How can this continue? I lived with her for two and a half months. Although there was no complete rupture, there was no deep affection either. From then on, I came to Nanjing, and two years have passed without me ever mentioning her. Now I am hesitating! If I were to divorce her, not only would my family not agree, but she would also be unwilling to leave me! In our area, the future for a woman like that is even more dangerous. If I don't divorce her, I will have to be a husband to a wooden puppet-like person for the rest of my life. Not only is there no happiness to speak of, but I also feel too unfulfilled to have courage! If I teach her to read, she is already older than me by four years, and I am six or seven thousand miles away. What should I do?

Answer: Your letter has been read and understood, and here is my reply: Your wife was not married freely, so naturally, it is unsatisfactory. In addition, she is "illiterate, does not understand human affairs, does not know the trends of the world, and knows even less about the true meaning of the union of men and women and of marriage," which makes you even more disappointed. However, let me say one thing, don't be offended. Illiteracy among women in the interior is a common phenomenon. Of course, girls in schools outside do not have this shortcoming, but it is difficult to say whether they "understand human affairs." In our experience, there are very few truly worldly fashionable women in the city, very few indeed! As for "not knowing the trends of the world, not knowing the true meaning of the union of men and women and of marriage," this shortcoming is by no means unique to your wife but is common among women in general, even among so-called female bachelors and doctors who graduated from universities and foreign countries. I am afraid that it is difficult to find someone who can clearly understand the trends of the world and deeply understand the union of men and women and the true meaning of marriage. Let me ask you a question in return: Have you tried to examine yourself and ask yourself: Do I truly know the trends of the world like the back of my hand? Do I truly have a thorough and complete understanding of the union of men and women and the true meaning of marriage? I am afraid that you would not dare to give an affirmative answer without the slightest hesitation. In that case, it is really too unforgiving to blame others for things that you cannot do yourself, to blame an ignorant and uneducated woman. We do not approve of your unreasonable blame. Our opinion is as follows: (1) Since your wife is very humble and obedient to you and filial to your parents, that is already rare in an old-fashioned woman. If it is because she is illiterate, then persuade her to come out to study. Fortunately, her parents are rich and will definitely be happy to cultivate her. As long as she comes out and experiences more, she will understand human affairs. This is not a problem. (2) We see the problem is still her age. She is a few years older than you. According to ordinary physiology, this is not very suitable; however, it is best if you first ask her to come out to study. When she arrives in a large city, sees more of the world, her knowledge will gradually become different, and her outlook on life will gradually change. Then, the things that you are not satisfied with her may gradually disappear, or at least be greatly reduced, or you may fall in love with her again. If the two of you ultimately cannot find common ground, explain the situation to her face. She will certainly not be as feudal-minded as before and consider divorce to be a disgrace to women. She can find her own suitable lover. You can then get rid of your shackles and "let the bird fly freely" and find your ideal woman! But I must also advise you: Don't set your sights too high. It is impossible to find a woman who is both worldly, knows the trends of the world, and deeply understands the true meaning of marriage. If there were such a woman, you would be satisfied, but I am afraid that you would not necessarily be her ideal man!

Important Education News

Spread of Student Protests in Northern Anhui 165

The Second Rural Normal School Vigorously Opposes Relocation to Suxian; Education Department Sends Personnel to Take Over but are Forced to Leave Bengbu

(Bengbu Correspondence) Zhu Tinghu, the Director of the Anhui Education Department, in order to implement educational cooperation and economize on educational funds, decided to close the Fourth Vocational School of Suxian County, relocate the Bengbu Second Rural Normal School to Suxian, and instruct the Seventh Vocational School here to manage the remaining site for the purpose of adding agricultural sciences. This series of twists and turns has caused many disputes, eventually leading to an uncontrollable student protest. The root cause is that the education authorities were too hasty in their actions. The relocation of the Second Rural Normal School to Suxian was opposed by the teachers and students of the school and local people in northern Anhui. The change of the school principal also led to problems, eventually resulting in events such as refusing the new principal to take over the school. It is understood that the original principal of the Second Rural Normal School, Ma Jingchang, who had studied in the United States, had good qualifications and was highly regarded by all parties. However, when the Education Department recently replaced a large number of secondary school principals, Ma was also among those dismissed and transferred to the province for reassignment. In addition, the fundamental relocation of the school to Suxian was the biggest reason for dissatisfaction among all parties in northern Anhui. Xu Huai, who was transferred to the position of principal of the Second Rural Normal School, was originally the principal of the Third Middle School in Fuyang. After Xu received the transfer order, he came to Bengbu to prepare for the takeover, but then, realizing that the atmosphere was bad and the environment was unfavorable, he quietly left Bengbu and resigned to the Education Department. The Education Department then telegraphed Wei Congxu, a provincial inspector who was staying in Bengbu on official business, to take over the school nearby. However, Wei also felt that the opposition at the school was fierce, and there was a so-called Anhui Northern Education Protection Association supporting them, so it was not appropriate to go there rashly. Even if he went to take over, it would be difficult to do so in practice. He then made an excuse to go elsewhere. Zhu Tinghu, the Director of the Education Department, found that it was impossible to take over the school for the time being, let alone relocate it. Such a long delay would undermine the administrative credibility of the Education Department. After repeated consideration, he sent Yang Xuekai, a provincial inspector from the department, to act as the principal of the Second Rural Normal School and ordered him to take over quickly. After receiving the order, Yang came to Bengbu and stayed at the East Asia Hotel, preparing to implement the takeover. The students of the school heard about it and immediately held an emergency meeting, deciding to oppose the takeover and posting fierce slogans on the streets, making explicit statements. The atmosphere of resistance to the Education Department was extremely high. The members of the Anhui Northern Education Protection Association also expressed their indignation upon hearing this. They first sent a letter to Yang to question him strictly, asking him which school and which person he was representing, and demanding an immediate reply. On the 9th, they met with Yang in full and advised him not to provoke public anger, to return to the province as soon as possible, so as to avoid the expansion of the unrest. Yang did not listen and instead accused the committee members of not interfering in educational administration and opposing the orders of the Education Department, saying that he had to take over this time. The representatives then left in anger. When the students of the Second Rural Normal School heard about it, they gathered a large number of people and went directly to Yang's residence, demanding that Yang not take over the school until the relocation issue was resolved, otherwise, they would ask him to return to the province immediately. Yang initially rebuked the students, but seeing the seriousness of the situation, he knew that it was difficult to stay. He had no choice but to agree to the students' request and was willing to return to the province immediately. He then quietly left Bengbu on the fifth train in the afternoon and returned to the province to report his mission. Since Yang was forced to leave, Wei Congxu, the provincial inspector who was negotiating with various parties in Bengbu, also expressed his indignation at the student unrest and decided to return to the province within days to report everything to the Education Department. According to the latest situation, the students of the Second Rural Normal School have stood in opposition to the Education Department. If the Education Department does not withdraw its decision to relocate to Suxian, this great student unrest may be difficult to resolve for a while.

Jiangsu Education Department Organizes Primary School Curriculum Compilation Committee 169

▲The First Meeting Will Be Held in Zhenjiang on the 16th of This Month

In order to compile kindergarten and primary school curricula, the Jiangsu Education Department has specially hired experts Wu, Yan Yin, Chen Heqin, Ge Chengxun, Gong Jia Yan, and others, as well as field researchers Ma Ketan, Shi Renfu, Sheng Langxi, Shen Yushan, Shen Shanzhi, Shen Shoujin, Jin Yingyuan, Pan Ren, and others. It has also designated several department staff members as committee members and will organize a committee to begin work immediately. The committee regulations and compilation methods have been drafted and the first meeting will be held in the Education Department on the morning of the 16th of this month. The compilation methods are recorded below:

▲Jiangsu Provincial Education Department's Methods for Compiling Kindergarten and Primary School Curricula (1) Organizing the Committee: In order to comply with the Ministry's order and compile kindergarten and primary school curricula, the department has specially invited experts and several field researchers, and has designated several department staff members to organize a compilation committee to handle the matter. (2) Scope of Compilation: Based on the Ministry's requirements for kindergarten and primary school curriculum standards and the operational requirements for each subject and each academic year, concrete teaching material outlines and teaching examples will be compiled. (3) Implementation Procedures: Five steps will be taken. The first step is to hold the first committee meeting in mid-March to discuss and compile implementation methods. At the same time, the subjects to be drafted will be identified separately, and the teaching material outlines will be drafted and submitted to the meeting by the end of April. The second step is to convene the second committee meeting in early May to review the outlines and determine the central units that can represent the subject matter in each group. The original drafters will then compile teaching examples for each subject separately and submit them to the meeting by the end of May. The third step is to compile and print the compilation outlines and examples for each subject, send them to the committee members for signing, and reply to the meeting before June 20. The fourth step is to convene the third committee meeting in early July to discuss and organize the methods, and at the same time, organize and complete the report to the Education Department for submission to the Ministry of Education for review and filing. The fifth step is to have the Education Department print and distribute the approved curricula to each primary school and kindergarten for trial implementation, and designate several schools to submit the results of the trial implementation to the department for review within a specified period, so as to revise them. (4) Compilation Methods: 1. In order to facilitate the compilation of the curriculum, the following seven groups will be established: (A) Kindergarten Group, (B) Primary School Chinese Language Group, (C) Primary School Arithmetic Group, (D) Primary School Physical Education Group, (E) Primary School Music Group, (F) Primary School Art and Manual Arts Group, (G) Primary School Social Studies, Natural Science, and Hygiene Group. 2. Each committee member will be responsible for one or two groups. Each group will have one committee member as the main drafter, and the other committee members should participate as much as possible in providing opinions and materials. 3. Each group should formulate complete (suitable for cities) and simplified (suitable for rural areas) concrete teaching material outlines and teaching examples in accordance with the fourth and seventh items of the curriculum standards implementation methods. 4. Each regulation should strive for communication to avoid the drawbacks of division, mixing, and repetition. (5) Points to Note: 1. Regarding the compilation of teaching material outlines: (A) The compilation of outlines should be based on the number of teaching hours for each subject in the curriculum standards, and should be divided by grade and semester. (B) The compilation of outlines should be suitable for the objectives of each subject in the curriculum standards and the operational requirements for each academic year. (C) The compilation of outlines should be concrete and representative. (D) The compilation of outlines should take into account the conditions of this province. (E) The compilation of outlines should take into account children's psychology, social conditions, and national needs. (F) In addition to knowledge and skills, the compilation of outlines should also take into account aspects such as spirit, habits, attitudes, and skills. (G) The compilation of outlines should be accompanied by the minimum necessary teaching equipment. 2. Regarding the compilation of teaching examples: (A) Teaching examples should be compiled separately for four groups: (A) Kindergarten, (B) Lower Primary School, (C) Middle Primary School, (D) Upper Primary School. (B) Education examples should be suitable for curriculum standards, kindergarten education methods, and general primary school teaching principles, and the teaching points of each subject.

The Completion of Shandong University Science Museum, Reorganized from Qingdao University 170

The Heads of the Shandong Education Department and Construction Department Went to Attend

(Jinan Quick News) Zhang Honglie, the Director of the Construction Department of the Shandong Provincial Government, and He Siyuan, the Director of the Education Department, took the second train of the Jiaoji Railway from Jinan at 10:00 PM on the 10th and went to Qingdao. It is said that they went to attend the completion ceremony of the Shandong University Science Museum. Since Qingdao University was reorganized into Shandong University, it has been greatly reorganized and has achieved excellent results. The school recently built a science museum, which is grand in scale and now fully equipped. The school previously sent letters to the Ministry of Education and Han Fuju, the Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, inviting them to attend the ceremony. Han Fuju was too busy with official duties to attend, so he sent Zhang Honglie, the Director of the Construction Department, to attend as a representative. Zhu Jiahua, the Minister of Education, also sent a telegram appointing He Siyuan, the Director of the Shandong Education Department, to attend as a representative nearby. According to Zhang Honglie, he will go to Qingdao to attend the completion ceremony of the Shandong University Science Museum and plans to leave Qingdao on the evening of Monday (the 13th) and return west. He also plans to inspect the construction situation in Jimo, Gaomi, and other counties along the way. According to He Siyuan, the Director of the Education Department, he will go to Qingdao to attend the completion ceremony of the Shandong University Science Museum and will go and return with Director Zhang (Honglie). If Director Zhang goes to Jimo, Gaomi, and other counties to inspect the construction situation, he will also go to the two counties to inspect the education situation.

Twenty-Nine Directors, Including Lin Sen, Were Elected

Special Lecture Agreements for Academic Lectures at the Municipal Education Hall 173

▲Letters Sent to Various Schools and Institutions to Solicit Listeners

The Shanghai Municipal Public Education Hall regularly holds academic lectures to explore academic issues. It has been operating for more than half a year. The details of the process are detailed in the first collection of academic lectures. Recently, it has been felt that the mobility of the listeners is limited and it is not easy to obtain a systematic concept. Therefore, a further plan has been made to send letters to various schools and institutions in the city to solicit 200 special listeners, so that they can have the opportunity to supplement their knowledge outside of class. The following methods have been established: 1. The purpose of the hall is to use lectures by various experts to provide for the needs of the general public with more knowledge. 2. The number of special listeners is tentatively set at 200. 3. Special listeners are not limited by age or gender. 4. Special listeners must have a junior high school education or above, and the list of names must be submitted by various schools or institutions to the hall. After review and approval, the hall will issue listening certificates. However, the number of people sent by each school or group must not exceed ten. 5. Those who have a junior high school education or above but are not students or work in institutions may also be special listeners for the hall's academic lectures. However, they must submit a clear resume to the hall for review and approval, and a listening certificate will be issued. 6. The hall's academic lectures are held once every two weeks. The date and topic of the lecture will be published in the education news section of major newspapers in the city one week before the lecture. 7. Special listeners are entitled to the following rights: (1) When the hall holds academic lectures, they may enter with their special listening certificate. (2) They may submit written inquiries about various issues related to academic lectures. (3) They have the right to suggest that the hall hire a certain lecturer. (4) They will be given the hall's publications. 8. Special listeners should fulfill the following obligations: (1) Respond to the hall's inquiries and investigations. (2) Publish their research findings in the hall's various publications. 9. Special listeners should abide by the following disciplines: (1) Do not leave the lecture midway. (2) If they are absent without reason three times, the hall may reclaim the listening certificate and replace it with a candidate. 10. These methods may be revised at any time.

The Municipal Education Bureau Sends Personnel to Investigate the Organizational Status of Various Primary Schools 174

▲Additional Classes Will Be Added After the Investigation is Completed

After the start of the second semester of the 21st academic year, the number of students in municipal primary schools in various districts has increased sharply, and they have successively requested the addition of classes. The Municipal Education Bureau of this city believes that it is necessary to open up more classrooms since the classrooms in various schools cannot accommodate them, but it is necessary to first understand whether the organization is completely appropriate and how many students there are in order to approve them. Previously, special personnel were sent to various schools to conduct a thorough investigation and fill out forms for reporting and review. It is now known that the investigation has been completed and a decision will be made to add classes as appropriate.

The Third Day of Wang Jiyuan's Painting Exhibition 175

Yesterday was the third day of Wang Jiyuan's painting exhibition. Artists from China and abroad came and went to the gatehouse of the French Association on Huanlong Road in an endless stream. Especially the young male and female students from various universities and art schools crowded into Wang's painting exhibition, observing and exploring, as if they were in the Louvre Museum in Paris. Wang's watercolor paintings are considered to be unique in the contemporary era. The large-format picture printed by the China Book Company was also published yesterday, and it is exceptionally exquisite. Guests such as writers Wang Lixi, Zhang Yiping, Lin Gengbai, Mr. and Mrs. Liu Yazi, Jin Shizi, Gu Jia Guanbaiyi, Gu Dingmei, Teng Gu, painters Liu Haisu and his wife, Ni Taide, Zhang Xian, journalists Huang Tianpeng, Xu Zexiang, educators Pan Gongzhan, Liu Suijiu, and others praised Wang's works, saying that the magic lies in the combination of Chinese and Western styles, and that he has discovered what previous people have not discovered, which is truly rare and valuable.

The Shanghai Municipal Council Normal School Opens 176

The normal school run by the Shanghai Municipal Council for English teachers has opened in Yucai Public School on Shanhai Pass Road. The school has now opened. In addition to students from the bureau's various schools who come here for tutoring, more than half of the students this semester are external students. There are still a few places available in each class. Those who wish to enroll may contact the head teacher of the school as soon as possible. The school's courses include the theory and practice of teaching methods, psychology, English conversation, English composition, English literature translation, and English subject teaching methods. The lecturers are mostly Western teachers from various schools. Among the students, in addition to Chinese, there are Germans, Indians, Russians, and Filipinos.

German People Oppose Hitler's Abandonment of the World Games 189

▲ German Sports Association Has Already Prepared for the Games

(Berlin Correspondence) German Chancellor Hitler once expressed opposition to Germany hosting the next World Games, his reason being that Germany's economic situation made it inconvenient to waste money on this again, and the platform of the National Socialist Party (i.e., the current ruling party) also opposed competitive sports and supported mass sports. Unexpectedly, after this proposal was made, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini announced that if Germany was willing to abandon the next World Games, he would be willing to accept the next Games to be held in Rome. Therefore, German public opinion was in an uproar, and the general public criticized Hitler's dictatorship. The opposition to competitive sports by the National Socialist Party has gradually subsided. The president of the German Sports Association, Lewald, in order to urge the national sports community to pay attention to the next Games, has recently been actively preparing for the affairs and often convenes meetings of the entire preparatory committee to achieve the best possible results for the next Games. The Games has now created a logo and distributed it to various countries for publicity.

Special Delivery

Preface to "New Key to Chinese Translation of Medical Terms" by Song Guobin 198

The rise of a word, the origin of a term, must have its source, and its process of development. Xu Shu Chong's description of the "Shuo Wen Jie Zi" says, "The word means to give birth and multiply and tilt more." Since it is said to give birth and multiply, each has its source. Since it is said to tilt more, it is said to increase. Is this only true of Chinese characters? In general, science has specialized scientific terms. The development of science is new every day and different every month, the breeding of terms, self-layered and endless, in this to the vast scientific terms, what will be the art to manage it? I have devoted myself to medicine for nearly 20 years, and I am always troubled by the complexity of terms and the difficulty of memorizing them. I thought about it and thought about it, thinking that I am not the only one who suffers from this. I then made up my mind to investigate and explore its roots, so that in the midst of grasping the main points, I could imply the meaning of simplifying the complex, for the convenience of my classmates and colleagues. Thus, this compilation was made. When studying the origin of European medical terms, there are Greek and Latin origins, of which 70% originate from Greek and 30% originate from Latin (anatomical terms mostly originate from Latin, while other medical terms mostly come from Greek). The structure of terms is divided into single words and compound words, with single words accounting for 30% and compound words accounting for 70%. Compound words have roots, prefixes, and suffixes. The meaning of the name varies depending on whether it comes from the prefix, suffix, or the connection between the prefix and suffix. Knowing its roots, prefixes, and suffixes makes the meaning of the whole word clear. This compilation is based on this, so it is divided into two parts, prefix and suffix (word roots and prefixes are prefixes, word roots and suffixes are suffixes), and all compound medical terms are classified within the prefix and suffix parts. Several examples are given as illustrations, with attached translations for reference. My humble intention is not to dare to boast of innovation, but to believe that reading Hua's books is based on literacy, and translating books is based on translating words. A word has a true meaning, and losing it by a hair's breadth can lead to a difference of a thousand miles. If one understands the origin from which it comes, it is like Yang Youji shooting fleas, without missing an ounce. Using it to read books will not be vague, and using it to translate can be accurate. New words are added every day, and scholars who check dictionaries often suffer from incompleteness. If they do not understand the key to literacy and beg for help from incomplete dictionaries, how can they have the joy of solving problems easily and having everything at their fingertips? Moreover, words are created by people, and the structure and meaning of the created words may not be consistent. Holding this secret key as a standard can not only examine and correct the original text, but also create new words, and is it only limited to literacy and translation? In recent years, the translation community in China has been very divided on scientific terms. The reason for the errors lies in the lack of clarity of the true meaning, and especially in the lack of knowledge of the origin of the words. Therefore, I have compiled this compilation, not considering my shallowness, so that scholars can follow this method to treat all scientific terms, and perhaps achieve twice the result with half the effort, and achieve the effect of unifying translation names. Its influence may not be limited to medical terms.
