Spring and Autumn

The Period of "No Solution" 199

— Baihe

—Dawn Still Awaits—

In the past, Europe had a "Dark Ages" and a "Renaissance," both of which were very important in history. But in this era, this world of unknown depths has stepped into a "no solution" period of 120% severity. Everyone scratched their heads and ears, and finally racked their brains, but there was no solution.

The old gentleman of the League of Nations, with the eyebrows and eyes of a gentleman, kept saying that Japan should spit out the Northeast and retreat its troops into the railway zone. Japan did not follow the order. What is the solution? Country A was afraid that Country B would have a powerful military and be threatened, so it very cleverly launched arms reduction. But people are not fools. You say arms reduction, I say equal armament. Using your spear to attack your shield, what is the solution? Due to the increasing severity of the unemployment problem, it is inevitable that there is a danger of economic revolution. Everyone finds economic revolution terrifying, but the unemployment problem cannot be solved after all. What is the solution? No one wants to cause a world war, because everyone has tasted the taste of the European War and feels that the matter of bloodshed is ultimately painful. But you want to seize my rights, I want to break your lifeline, red eyebrows facing green eyes, and insist on not taking the path of world war. What is the solution? Killing someone pays with your life, owing money pays it back. This is a matter of course and inescapable. But the debtor keeps delaying with tears and snot, intending to deny the debt. What is the solution? Under the oppression of imperialism, the colonies gradually see through the paper tiger of imperialism, resist with great sacrifices, and rise up in resistance. When the imperialists' poison gas cannons cannot suppress the revolutionary sentiments, what is the solution for the imperialists?

The modern recession has enveloped the entire world. We Chinese really have no solution. Countries around the world are also clamoring for no solution. "The long night is long, and dawn still awaits." This "no solution" period is probably not easy to get through.

"Entertainment" and "Saving the Nation" 200

— Ke Ding'an

Our China, every time after going through a national crisis,

, it is as if we have had an injection, temporarily excited, but ultimately silent. Since the recent September 18th Incident, the effect of that injection has been relatively long, but the sons of wealthy families who are drunk in the sounds and colors of horses and dogs are still like this, but they also learn from the enthusiastic people and say:

"Entertainment saves the nation"!

If entertainment can really save the nation, then "eating" and "sleeping" can also save the nation. What a bizarre saying!

Based on the principle of entertainment saving the nation, General ××, when his homeland was full of artillery fire, still wanted to indulge in singing and musical rhythms in the old city. This is putting "entertainment saving the nation" into practice!

"Can't entertainment really save the nation?" Someone asked me this. I said:

"Entertainment can also save the nation, but you have to change the way a little bit to suit the original meaning of entertainment saving the nation. If you have friends coming, you want to invite them to see a play. According to the most ordinary expenses, two people would have to spend three yuan. You should donate these three yuan. At the same time, you can explain to your friends that I was originally going to invite you to see a play today, but because I was moved by patriotism, I would rather take the three yuan to donate to the Northeast. I think you and I are equally patriotic and will certainly agree."

I think "a heart of patriotism, something everyone possesses"! If you say this to your friend, your friend doesn't need to say anything, he will definitely agree, and he will admire you very much!

There are so many entertainment venues in Shanghai, such as Beijing opera houses, movie theaters, amusement parks, massage parlors, ballrooms, book stalls, and other secret places that I can't name or call. If we Chinese can all do it in my way, "using hot blood and heat" (Note), the result is really not something that can be described in a few words. When this method can be implemented, it will be the day when the Republic of China will turn over.

Isn't it time for "aviation saving the nation"? If the Chinese in Shanghai can implement my method of "entertainment saving the nation", then the success of "aviation saving the nation" is not far away.

Note: Hot blood and heat cannot be separated, so I use them together.

The Relativity of Beauty 201

— A Tang

"Beauty" is relative, not absolute. Humans, and it can be said that various animals, have different aesthetic concepts due to various relationships.

Chickens, dogs, and pheasants on the mountain, in the eyes of humans, the males are certainly more beautiful than the females, but in the world of living things, repulsion between the same sex and attraction between different sexes is a certain principle. Therefore, in the minds of male chickens, dogs, and pheasants themselves, the females are probably not as ugly as humans feel. Otherwise, why would the males pursue the females? Would you pursue an ugly woman in your mind?

The indigenous women of Africa, in the eyes of civilized humans, are of course extremely ugly; but in the perceptions of the indigenous people of Africa, they must be very beautiful.

Old gentlemen in their sixties and seventies, when they see modern women, some will shake their heads and sigh, saying! "Now the world is really getting worse, the young girls are dressed up in an unseemly way." This is because of the physiological decline of the elderly; second, because the trends of their youth are different, so their aesthetic concepts are also different from those of young people now. I think when they were young, they were also passionately pursuing women with bound feet and morbid beauty.

Without climbing high mountains, you cannot see flat ground. What you have always considered to be the most beautiful will definitely be diminished in value after you discover something even more beautiful, and this has caused a lot of fluctuations in the world.

Therefore, there is no fixed standard for the so-called "beauty" in the world.

National Crisis and Women 204

— Ju Yun

The pass has fallen! The invaders are deep in our territory! A great war is about to break out! But among women, there will be no shortage of Hua Mulan, who joined the army in place of her father, and Qin Liangyu, who loyally defended the emperor and suppressed the bandits. Perhaps we have seen on stage and in historical novels: "Riding a peach blossom horse, wielding a nine-dragon blade, the female general is awe-inspiring, taking the lead, fighting the bandits for hundreds of rounds."

Even now, we see many! Female military officers, wearing high leather boots, full military uniform, and armed belts, are just as heroic and high-spirited; their gun barrels aim at the enemy's vital point, "one person guarding the pass, ten thousand cannot pass." Kill one for every one that comes, even if the Japanese devils could escape to the heavens!

Although only a small portion of women can do this, haven't the majority of sisters and aunts in cities and villages had equally important roles and tasks: "Rearguard work"?

During the last European war, European women were able to endure hardship and did many great and amazing things:

They rescued wounded soldiers brought back from the front lines and supplied food and weapons to the brave warriors at the front; in order to maintain the safety of local municipalities, they organized well-equipped female police forces and female defense corps: the financial and commercial sectors, which could not be abandoned at any time, all needed women in "agriculture," "industry," and "commerce."

The abilities of Chinese women are no less than those of others. Why shouldn't we be as good as European women? Then we might as well close our eyes and think for a moment. It seems that every woman will carry a heavy burden from now on!

But looking back at some of the sisters in the cities, they are still only concerned with dressing up beautifully, watching movies, playing mahjong, and wasting some boring time, without ever thinking that the enemy has already entered the door of our house!

Or perhaps the sisters in the Pingjin area have already felt deep terror, hurriedly fleeing south, seeking temporary safety.

Only those who are in the southern provinces or have arrived in the southern provinces think they can relax and be carefree for a while, leading a carefree and happy life; they have made no preparations, and they have no awareness!

We still cannot forget the ruins left by the January 28th Incident in Shanghai!

Everyone has already learned about the violent and heinous acts of the Japanese bandits.

Is it really necessary for the enemy to kill us before our eyes before we wake up? I don't think women are that stupid!

I know very well that if there is a thief, he doesn't even need to carry any weapons, at most a bright, sharp knife. If he visits the home of any sister, nine out of ten will only be frightened and tremble, without any idea of what to do.

In fact, terror and shrinking back are of no use! Naturally, if you have made sufficient preparations for everything, you will not be flustered in an emergency.

The practical exercises and efforts needed now are a matter of "life and death," and there is no room for further hesitation or delay.

We have also seen that many "women's associations," which represent women's groups, have already started working, and they are also proposing to raise funds to purchase a "Women's Plane" to realize the current popular idea of saving the country through aviation.

According to the calculation of 200 million female compatriots, it seems that buying a plane does not take much effort. On average, even if each person donates one cent, two million can be raised. Thirteen or fourteen planes would be easy to obtain, and each woman only needs to save three copper coins.

Then the modern ladies can buy one less cosmetic, buy one less new outfit, watch one less movie, and get their hair permed one less time. The Buddhist wives can take out half of the incense offered before the Buddha, and the family can eat less meat for a few days, which is equally meritorious. Sisters who make a living by sewing can work a little harder for half a night and save some national salvation savings. Those with good reputations can stop for a while. If you can donate all the money you planned to use for gambling, you might save a lot of money, at least enough to avoid owing a dollar here and a few cents there.

When you are free, you can be free, but when "national crisis is at hand" and "the pain cuts deep," people in the same boat should no longer have a life of leisure and complacency!
