— Pang Jingzhou

Chapter 4: Business Conditions

(Note) The Shanghai Public Hospital in the Nanshi area, mentioned in the previous article, used to admit epidemic patients during the epidemic period. However, the new building for the epidemic department of the hospital has now been completed, and the equipment has been greatly improved, so it can now accept patients with major infectious diseases all year round. In addition, the Zhabei Public Hospital has also been rebuilt and improved after the war. These two news are good news for the citizens of Shanghai.

Now let's talk about the individual businesses in the new medical community. We have already said that the total number of new doctors in Shanghai is not considered small when compared to the number of people. However, because people in society tend to favor traditional Chinese medicine, the business of each new doctor is not very developed on average. It is natural that competition in business forces them to use some business tactics. Business tactics are nothing more than catering to the psychology of society. If we say that expressing harmony, kindness, and friendliness in the words and actions of responding to patients does not shake the status and academic knowledge of the doctor, it is also the attitude that every practicing doctor in the world should take. However, in China, it is sometimes very difficult to be harmonious. For example, if a patient hires both a new and old doctor and asks the new doctor to consider the prescription of the old doctor, asking whether he should take it or not? Or ask if there are any disadvantages to taking both Chinese and Western medicine at the same time? This kind of question really makes it impossible for the new doctor to answer. The most honest and non-deceptive answer is the word "I don't know." As a result, the patient complains that the new doctor is uneducated and has no responsible answer. Under such difficult circumstances, new doctors with great reputations often abandon the patient and use "please hire someone more skilled" as a way out, but his colleagues who criticize him can also accuse him of "irresponsibility" or "becoming like a traditional doctor," but I have carefully considered this situation and decided that it is by no means something that either the doctor or the patient can create. As for the lower-level business tactics, it is inevitable that they will be speculative. For example, whichever disease is most common in society, that disease is used as a topic to attract business. Like Shanghai today, it is a city with difficult living conditions and a decadent atmosphere, so there are many people suffering from venereal diseases and neurasthenia. As a result, the signs for brain and sexual disease clinics spring up like mushrooms after rain, and frustrated businessmen and absurd young people flock to them. Lung disease is a major enemy of the whole world, especially in big cities, so there are many in Shanghai. It is really as funny as brain and sexual diseases for non-experts to call themselves lung disease experts. In my opinion, Shanghai has special epidemics in all seasons, so doctors with a little bit of a thick skin might as well become experts who change with the seasons: in spring, they are called diphtheria and scarlet fever experts; in April and May, they are called measles and pediatric experts; in summer, they are called cholera and diarrhea experts; and in autumn, they are called dysentery and malaria experts; it is not impossible! The new medical association recently decided to restrict the advertisements of formal doctors and not allow them to falsely claim subjects. Even if they are real experts, they must meet the standard of having a major in this field in the medical academic system, which is a very proper method. Practicing doctors can be roughly divided into two categories: one is the one who rules all subjects; the other is the specialist. Specialists are naturally in the minority, and those who rule all subjects naturally account for the majority. In theory, all general practitioners should introduce the patient to a specialist for treatment due to academic and equipment reasons when encountering difficult and complicated symptoms. However, in Shanghai today, it has not yet reached this level. Except for a small number of people with great knowledge and great assets who seek medical treatment from experts, others only seek medical treatment from general practitioners. Because their business is not very developed, general practitioners may not be able to give up business and introduce serious illnesses to experts one by one. (According to regulations, formal doctors must pass all subjects before they are allowed to practice. Minor illnesses in all subjects can be treated.) Moreover, is Shanghai's experts in all subjects complete? Is it good or not? It is still a question, so it is actually difficult to do, and the patient's knowledge and economic strength, whether they can all be treated by experts? It also matters. The three things I have personally experienced can be used as proof of this statement: (1) Once I accidentally relieved the considerable pain of a hemorrhoid patient, he introduced many hemorrhoid patients, thinking that I was a hemorrhoid expert. In fact, hemorrhoids alone are not listed as a specialty, and I am not a hemorrhoid expert, but as a result, I gained considerable experience, and a part of the most difficult patients were still introduced to other places; (2) Once, a patient's family hired an old doctor to treat malaria, but they insisted on asking me to introduce a Western doctor who specializes in treating malaria. There is no specialty for malaria consultations, so I had to introduce an internist to them in a harmonious way; (3) A patient's wife insisted on a foreign female doctor to perform an ultra-superior abdominal surgery, saying that it seemed indecent for a man to perform the surgery, so I had to decline by saying "there is no such thing in Shanghai." (End of this chapter)

On Phlegm, Part 4 207

— Yu Yunxiu

Then, is it impossible to understand the old medical theory of phlegm disease? I say, analyze it! The way to analyze it is to first rectify the names. If the names are rectified, then all diseases can be classified according to their types, so that they will not be wandering souls without a home, living together in a mixed manner. Now, let's temporarily define those that are viscous and sticky as phlegm and those that are clear and thin as drink, according to the old medical terms of modern times. Then, what the old doctors call phlegm is the mucus that today's scientific medicine calls mucus. There are two places in the human body that produce mucus: one is the epithelial cells, and the other is the connective tissue. Those produced by epithelial cells are called epithelial cell mucus, and those produced by connective tissue are called connective tissue mucus. Epithelial cell mucus is produced from mucous membranes and mucous glands. The human body's skin has mucous membranes and mucous glands that can secrete mucus, such as the mouth, nose, throat, trachea, esophagus, stomach, intestines, urethra, cervix, and the Eustachian tube in the ear. Connective tissue mucus is in the joint membrane, synovial bursa, tendon sheath, and the umbilical cord of the fetus, and the subcutaneous tissue in the early stages of fetal life is also mucus.

Within the scope of physiology, there are places with mucous membranes and mucous glands that often secrete a small amount of mucus, such as the small intestine and cervix. There are also those that never secrete mucus, such as the nose and trachea. When there is disease, those that secrete a small amount become a large amount, such as the stool during dysentery and the cervical leukorrhea. Those that do not secrete become secretory, such as nasal mucus and turbid saliva. There are also places without mucus cells that cannot produce mucus, but become producing liquid mucus, such as mucus cancer. Therefore, in pathology, any place that does not secrete mucus but secretes mucus, and any place that secretes a small amount but secretes a large amount, can be called "mucus degeneration." Then, in a broad sense, all diseases of mucus degeneration can be called phlegm diseases. The most obvious ones are various mucositis, such as nasal catarrh, pharyngeal catarrh, tracheal, bronchial, esophageal, gastric, intestinal, urethral, and cervical catarrh, all are phlegm diseases. The causes of inflammation of the mucous membranes in various places are various chemical and physical stimuli, and various bacteria, such as influenza bacteria, diphtheria bacteria, tuberculosis, syphilis, gonococcus, cholera bacteria, and dysentery bacteria. It is not caused by the seven emotions, six excesses, overwork, or diet.

In addition, mucus edema, mucus tumor, and various mucus mixed tumors, mucus cancer, and ovarian cystic tumors are also all phlegm diseases.

In addition, the mucus temporarily secreted in the trachea and esophagus during acute neurological disorders, such as stroke and epilepsy, and that produced during heart failure, is considered by old doctors to be wind-phlegm and shock-phlegm. However, these secretions are mostly serous and belong to drink diseases, which are closer. Calling them phlegm diseases is not really relevant. Moreover, these secretions are produced after stroke and epilepsy, not because there is phlegm first and then the disease develops.

The above are what I call phlegm in a broad sense. As for the phlegm that the world calls cough phlegm, etc., it refers specifically to the mucus secreted in the respiratory organs, which the ancients called turbid saliva and saliva. I call it phlegm in a narrow sense.

However, whether it is phlegm in a broad sense or phlegm in a narrow sense, the essence of the disease is in different places and does not belong to the same category. The causes of the disease are also in different places and do not belong to the same category. The common phenomenon is that mucus is produced. Mucus is produced after there is disease. It is a product of the disease, not the main body of the disease. Therefore, today's science, although it knows that several diseases can produce mucus, there is no possibility and necessity to establish a special "mucus disease" name. This can be understood from the above. However, the name "phlegm disease" of old doctors is very unreasonable, and those who organize the national heritage should cut it out and discard it.

As for the symptoms caused by phlegm, in nasal mucositis, there are headaches, nasal congestion, and speech sounds like in a jar. However, whether the headache of nasal catarrh is meningeal congestion or serous inflammation is still an unresolved issue. In short, it is the influence of mucositis, not the influence of the mucus it secretes. In ear Eustachian tube inflammation, there is hearing loss, in trachea and bronchitis, there is cough, asthma, and shortness of breath, in the pharynx, there is nausea, in the stomach, there is bloating and loss of appetite, in the intestines, there is diarrhea, in the anterior yin, there is gonorrhea and leukorrhea and prostatic leakage, in the joints, there is joint swelling and pain, and in the subcutaneous tissue, there is mucus edema. Various symptoms are also in different places and do not belong to the same category. They should all be classified under various diseases, so that the analysis is clear and there is no danger of confusion. Do not establish a "phlegm disease" category and collect all the mucus

The Advantages and Disadvantages of Consulting a Doctor by Mail 208

— Song Guobin

In order to eliminate the difficulty for patients in the inland to have no doctor when they are sick and to solve the difficulty for poor patients to have no ability to seek medical treatment when they are sick, various new and old pharmaceutical publications have specially opened a column for medical and pharmaceutical consultation to give patients the convenience of consulting a doctor by mail. Especially the medical and pharmaceutical supplements in various daily newspapers.

In addition to the above two simple opinions, there are two important meanings: (1) to widely publicize medical and pharmaceutical knowledge in order to achieve the popularization of medical and pharmaceutical knowledge; (2) to publicly study difficult and complicated issues.

This cannot be regarded as a gospel for mankind! But after careful investigation, how much dangerous nature is contained in this gospel of mankind. Now, from the perspective of medical treatment and prescription itself, there are the following two questions.

Aren't we eliminating the difficulty for patients in the inland to have no doctor when they are sick and solving the difficulty for poor patients to have no ability to seek medical treatment when they are sick? But when we open the newspaper, are all those who ask for medical treatment from the inland and poor? This really gives patients a cunning and stingy opportunity to not seek medical treatment when they are sick! The patient thinks that a piece of empty paper can get a therapeutic solution, and a very limited number of postage stamps can exchange for the safety of his life and the disappearance of pain. Is there such a cheap thing in the world? Since there are not completely no doctors in the inland and those who ask for medical treatment are not completely poor, with such a cheap opportunity for patients, the practicing doctors in the inland are invisibly suffering a major loss, and the editors of our faithful medical and pharmaceutical publications are also invisibly being used by cunning patients!

Doctors have a great responsibility to patients. No matter how big or small the disease is, doctors must go through precise on-site examinations before they can have accurate diagnoses and prescriptions. Therefore, diagnosing diseases cannot be based entirely on the patient's verbal reports. As for what is written on paper, it is even less reliable! In this kind of unpredictable disease condition, giving a therapeutic answer based on a letter from the patient is, of course, that the patient's report is not completely consistent with the disease condition, even if it is completely consistent, and in this kind of question and answer back and forth, the disease condition may have undergone special changes. The patient does not know that there is danger, is the doctor not "loving it, but actually harming it"?

There is nothing in the world that has only advantages and no disadvantages, so consulting a doctor by mail is not absolutely impossible. What I hope for from the editors of medical and pharmaceutical publications is that they should take an extremely cautious attitude towards consulting a doctor by mail, so that the results obtained will not deviate from the original intention of benefiting mankind. In particular, there must be transparent observation so as not to be obscured by the patient and to harm the rights and interests of colleagues in the inland.

As for using this as a tool for personal publicity or selling foreign medicine, it is even less worth mentioning.

Page 16

Inflammation and all the symptoms of mucus degeneration, mixed and listed. As for the symptoms of neurasthenia, hysteria, etc. that have nothing to do with mucus, such as palpitations, fear of being caught, tinnitus, wind sounds behind the brain, etc., as well as the symptoms of bronchial secretions produced by stroke and epilepsy, etc., should not belong to phlegm, let alone be said to be caused by phlegm. They can be eliminated.

Now, let's talk about the nature of mucus. Mucus is a homogeneous, transparent, viscous liquid with traction. It can swell greatly when added to water. It dissolves in alkaline liquid. When acetic acid or alcohol is added to its solution, it precipitates like clouds. It is red when stained with Thionin and Muzinkramin. Its chemical essence is characterized by containing mucin. Mucin is a glycoprotein, which is a combination of protein and carbohydrates. Then, phlegm is a product of the body with special chemical properties. It is not made by accumulation of water and drink or stagnation of body fluids. It is clear.

Using Traditional Chinese Medicine in a Western Way (Continued) 209

— Zhou Mengbai

(8) Fennel (Small Fennel) Foeniculum.

(Origin) This product is the mature fruit of the plant of the Umbelliferae family, Small Fennel Foenicujum Vulgare Miller).

(Shape) This product is a double-hanging fruit, presenting a small long cylindrical shape, the outside presents a light greenish-yellow color, hairless, the top end has a remaining floral disc, the bottom end has a small fruit stem of about three or one-zero millimeters long, easily separated into two segments, each segment has five obvious rib-like lines on the back, and there is a wavy fuzzy secondary rib-like line between each rib-like line, the odor is special and pleasant, the taste is strong and sweet and fragrant.

(Ingredients) This product contains volatile oil, namely fennel oil, about 3% to 8%. The main components of this oil are Anethol, Terebin, and Fenchon. In addition, this product also contains fatty oil and sugar.

(Experiment) This product should not sink immediately when put into water or change the color of the water. Otherwise, it is a deoiled product or a product with added coloring. In addition, the produced extract should have 24% to 25%. If it does not reach this limit, it is an old product, a deoiled product, or a product mixed with similar fruits. The fragrance is also different. When fennel oil is shaken with alcohol, it should be clear and mixed. Otherwise, it is evidence of mixing other volatile oils and other fatty oils.

(Efficacy) This product is a stomachic, carminative, and expectorant drug. It is often used in a dose of 5 to 10 grams as an infusion. Its oil can also be used as a flavoring oil-sugar agent.

(Storage) The oil of this product gradually changes when exposed to air and sunlight, so it should be fully filled in small brown bottles, protected from sunlight, and sealed tightly.

(Appendix Old Saying) Pungent and mild, regulates qi, opens the stomach, and also treats cold hernia.

Scientific Methods of Achieving Longevity (8) 210

— Yu Songyun

(C) The Second Stage of Childbirth... Expulsion Stage

The labor pains in the second stage of childbirth are called labor pains in the expulsion stage. During this stage, the cervix has fully dilated, the amniotic sac has ruptured, and the baby's head has entered the vagina. Afterwards, the labor pains are specifically for expelling the fetus. At this time, the labor pains are severe and frequent, and last very long, often inducing reflexive abdominal pressure to help the baby's head advance.

During labor pains, the baby's head descends, and when the pain stops, it retreats. At that time, the perineum extends, the anus gapes open, and the rectal wall everts. Not only is there a bowel movement, but also stool leaks out, so that the labor pains become more severe and the perineum becomes more distended, presenting a spherical shape. A part of the baby's head opens the labia, and when the labor pains stop slightly, the baby's head retreats backwards, and the labia (cleft) closes again. The stronger the labor pains, the more the baby's head advances, so that the vulva is unusually tense. At this time, the pregnant woman is in severe pain, and her efforts become even greater. Suddenly, her face turns red, her eyes are bright, her lips are red-purple and dry, her pulse is frequent, and there are fine arterial pulsations on the tips of her fingers, which shows the tension of the whole body's exertion. At the same time, the whole body sweats. When the labor pains come again, the whole body trembles. At this time, even during the intervals of labor pains, the baby's head no longer retreats. It immediately appears outside the vulva, commonly known as the time when the top of the head is exposed. The tension of the external genitalia has reached its extreme, and the pregnant woman cannot bear the pain, shouting non-stop, and even losing consciousness. The baby's head is expelled at this time, or after two or three more labor pains, it can be completely produced. The fetus announces its birth in a cry.

(D) The Third Stage of Childbirth... Afterbirth Stage

After the fetus is born, the placenta and amniotic membrane are expelled after twenty or thirty minutes, or at the same time. However, when the placenta is expelled, afterbirth labor pains occur, specifically to make the uterus contract and squeeze out the placenta, presenting a spherical shape. Then, the childbirth ends from here.

▲ Reply to those who request abortion

Recently, I have received letters requesting abortion. It must happen several times a month. Although the reasons given are nothing more than physical weakness and inability to bear the burden of childbirth, I don't know that abortion is not only full of dangers, not less than a miscarriage, but also violates the criminal law. We doctors take humanitarianism as the foundation. Not only do I absolutely not allow myself to perform abortions for others, but I often warn society to avoid the dangers of abortion. If anyone disregards the danger and rashly aborts, it will violate the criminal law, destroy life, and cause the greatest harm. The criminal law of our country has repeatedly emphasized the punishment for abortion, but those who intend to try it still treat it as a dead letter. Here are the main points:

(1) A pregnant woman who takes medicine or uses other methods to abort shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not more than one year, detention, or a fine of not more than 300 yuan. The same shall apply to a pregnant woman who listens to others to abort. (Section 304)

(2) Anyone who causes a pregnant woman to abort at the request of the pregnant woman or with her consent shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not more than two years. Anyone who causes the death of the woman as a result shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not more than five years. (Section 305)

(3) Anyone who commits the crime in the first paragraph of the preceding article with the intention of making a profit shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not less than six months and not more than five years and may be fined not more than 500 yuan. (Section 306)

(4) Anyone who publicly introduces methods or items for abortion or publicly introduces their own or others' behavior of abortion in writing, pictures, or other methods shall be sentenced to imprisonment for not more than one year, detention, and may be fined or converted to a fine of not more than 1,000 yuan. (Section 308)

The above is just a brief reply. I will not reply to each letter in the future. I hope you understand. (End)

A Brief Discussion on Asthma 211

— Hou Guangdi

Asthma, known in the West as Asthma. The Greek word means "I am struck." The most prominent symptom of this condition is difficulty breathing, accompanied by a peculiar wheezing sound. The onset usually occurs around two in the morning. The patient suddenly wakes up, unable to breathe without propping themselves up with pillows. The wheezing gradually worsens, reaching a point where it seems as if they are on the verge of suffocation. Then, suddenly, they improve. Those who have suffered from this condition for a long time are accustomed to these alarming symptoms and are not greatly frightened. The onset of this condition is intermittent, but the intervals vary. Some cases are preceded by colds, bronchitis, or indigestion.

Mild asthma only involves difficulty breathing. Severe cases involve cold limbs, profuse sweating, and vomiting. After two or three hours, the condition gradually eases, and the patient coughs up sticky phlegm, finally returning to normal. At this point, the patient is extremely tired and falls into a peaceful sleep. The next day, the illness seems to have disappeared. However, most patients often suffer from bronchitis with coughing and excessive phlegm, and some suffer from indigestion.

Those who suffer from gout and are prone to eczema often also suffer from asthma. The two conditions often alternate. Excessive stomach acid, restlessness, and indigestion are common ailments associated with asthma. Syphilis and malaria can also commonly contribute to the suffering of asthma.

The cause of asthma is a matter of debate. Some attribute it to the blood, others to nervous system disorders. However, judging from the symptoms, it is clear that during an asthma attack, the constrictive center of the brain nerves triggers a constrictive action, causing the muscles around the bronchi to contract. The reason why the constrictive center acts in this way must be due to impurities in the blood.

In addition to these, there are various external causes, such as changes in air, dust, contact with flower pollen, the smell of birds and animals, the oily smells of cooking in the kitchen, and the spraying of perfume, all of which can trigger asthma. From this, it can be inferred that improper food is certainly one of the triggers. Therefore, those who have suffered from asthma for a long time can often identify certain unsuitable foods and avoid them to prevent the onset of the condition.

About 40% of cases of this condition are hereditary.

Treatment is divided into two types: radical and emergency. Radical treatment requires examining the patient for other underlying causes, such as syphilis, glandular disease, malaria, gout, diabetes, etc., and treating them to free the brain nerves from stimulation. Nasal fungus in the nasal cavity and throat moths in the throat are also causes of this condition and must be removed. For emergency treatment, the best option is to inject ephedrine or a combination of Atropine sulfate and morphine, or alternate injections of adrenaline. Burning Datura leaves soaked in saltpeter into black smoke and inhaling it often produces remarkable results.

Ephedrine is made from domestically produced ephedra. It has a special effect in treating asthma. It is available for injection and oral administration in various regions. Foreign pharmaceutical companies such as Moufu, Parke Davis, Eli Lilly, and Merck all produce it. The product manufactured by the New Asia factory is also very fine and has a faster effect. I have used it extensively and have never been disappointed. I highly recommend it to the people of our country.

A Visit to Hangzhou Minsheng Pharmaceutical Factory 212

— Chen Xiaomei

With the atmosphere of aggression intensifying daily and the national crisis deepening, at this critical juncture of survival, how can we find time for national salvation, let alone industry and resistance? However, Mr. Zhou Shiluo, at this time, did not forget industry in saving the nation. He worked tirelessly, day and night, sparing no effort, using his knowledge to establish the Minsheng Pharmaceutical Factory in Hangzhou, engaging in the manufacture of medicines, medical equipment, and glassware.

On the eve of the lunar New Year, I was invited by Mr. Lu Zhixue and Mr. Wu Guanmin to visit the factory. I had the opportunity to see Mr. Zhou's demeanor. I found Mr. Zhou to be kind and approachable. He guided us and explained everything in detail. What impressed us most was that the layout of the factory and the design of the equipment were all Mr. Zhou's own creations. For example, the furnace, stove, and chimney required for the steam boiler, and the structure of the gate, all utilized scientific principles to save fuel. For the filling of ampoules with liquid medicine, the principle of the air pump was used, allowing one thousand to one thousand plus ampoules to be filled per hour. Hangzhou has no gas, so kerosene lamps were used, with a hole in the middle and air blown in, the flame size can be adjusted as desired, the effect is like a Bunsen burner. Other examples include the use of a ball bladder to replace a bellows to pump air. Examples like these are too numerous to mention.

The factory is divided into three departments: the chemical pharmaceutical department, the medical equipment department, and the glassware department. It employs many experts to specialize in manufacturing. The following is a summary of the general situation of the factory:

(1) Chemical Pharmaceutical Department

Although the department does not have large-scale equipment, the machinery used in manufacturing is quite complete. Such as automatic tablet machines, mixing machines, pill machines, sugar coating machines, polishing machines, ointment grinding machines, etc., all of which are self-made. The injection medicine room is equipped with steam throughout, with vacuum distillation equipment, vacuum washing equipment, and ampoule filling equipment (made by Mr. Zhou). Male and female workers are trained, and all operations are well organized. The department has recently manufactured a new drug called Pityol to counter the foreign-made Pityrol. It will be displayed at the Chicago World's Fair.

(2) Medical Equipment Department

Because the workers in this department all went home for the New Year at the end of the lunar year, I was unable to visit, which is a great regret.

(3) Glassware Department

This department is equipped with a furnace, a vacuum pump, and an air storage tank. It specializes in manufacturing neutral hard glass, such as various sizes of ampoules, cowpox tubes, serum bottles, test tubes, injection tubes, measuring cups, medicine bottles, safety funnels, beakers, mortars, funnels, conical funnels, flasks, round-bottom flasks, etc. Although there are larger glass bottle factories at sea, the quality of their products cannot be compared to the excellence of this factory, this can be stated with certainty.

In addition, the most famous products of the factory include: Trypalin, Vertodin, Antihustin, Pityol, Oxytin, Gimenor, Salpalin, Plolnichin, Quinoblau, Fiberung, Digitolin, Magnol, and hundreds of others. I can hardly imagine how much effort Mr. Zhou has put into them! Mr. Zhou has recently been working hard to make further progress, striving for perfection. His diligent and hardworking professional attitude cannot be described in words. Mr. Zhou can be said to be a person with the will to save the country through industry!

The Social Mission of Doctors (4) 213

— Fan Shouyuan

▲▲▲……………………………………　…▲▲▲

In the past, when science was underdeveloped and medicine could not yet use scientific methods for research and experimentation, it was of course difficult to distinguish right from wrong and truth from falsehood. One could only guess and tell lies. In the modern era of advanced science, medicine has been able to use scientific methods for research and experimentation. Therefore, it is undoubtedly necessary to abandon the false and erroneous old medicine and apply the correct and reasonable scientific new medicine. However, the general public, having been subjected to past inherited propaganda for a long time, does not understand the errors and falsehoods of old medicine and unconsciously believes that these erroneous and false old medical theories are correct and reasonable. The unawakened old doctors, on the other hand, are unwilling to recognize the times, admit the backwardness of old medicine, and refuse to submit to the truth and admit the falsehood of old medicine. Instead, they actively propagate and spread rumors about these false pseudo-medical theories to society: running newspapers, running colleges, and organizing groups to carry out reactionary movements. On the one hand, the public is easily anesthetized and deceived by the lies of old medicine because of the inherited ideas left over from thousands of years in the past. On the other hand, old doctors take advantage of the weakness of the public's naive thinking and inherited minds to further exert their ability to deceive the masses. In fact, the result of this reactionary work is only to lead the public into a misguided path that is detrimental to health. Therefore, for the health of the public and the future of the country and the nation, we should shoulder the revolutionary work of opposing old medicine, analyze the falsehoods and fallacies of old medicine, explain them to the public, propagate them to the people, and change their past metaphysical minds and the errors of inherited thinking. It is necessary for the majority of the public to feel awakened to the errors of old medicine in the past in order to develop faith in scientific new medicine. Metaphysical minds and inherited thoughts will definitely not be able to accommodate the knowledge of scientific new medicine! It is even more difficult to correct the habit of spitting phlegm everywhere for a tuberculosis patient who does not believe that there are countless tuberculosis bacteria that can infect each other hidden in the phlegm. Our propaganda work of instilling medical knowledge into the public is for the purpose of improving the public's health. If we want the public to be able to accept and enjoy the benefits of this medical knowledge, we cannot avoid doing some destructive work against old medicine. The nature and significance of this revolutionary work of destroying old medicine is no less important than the two tasks mentioned above: saving the public from suffering and instilling medical knowledge! This major task, which is related to the future of the country, should not only be the task of a few new medical personnel, but the task of every new medical personnel, the task of all doctors in the new medical community! (The End)

Page 17

Economic Special Issue

What Will the Future Hold for the Gold Standard? (Part 1) 214

— Pan Shihao

▲ A Major Transformation Since 1816

The gold standard for currency truly began in England in 1816, after which various countries followed suit. Due to its fixed production and stable value, it was deemed the most suitable medium of exchange. In modern times, with the increasing convenience of transportation, the economic relationships between countries have become closely intertwined. The smooth functioning of international lending and settlements is largely due to the stability of the gold standard in various countries. When the European War broke out in 1914, many participating countries suspended the gold standard, but only regarded it as an emergency measure during wartime. Therefore, after the peace treaty was concluded, they restored it one after another. People generally regarded the gold standard as a canal for connecting international economies and even considered it the supreme standard for currency.

In 1929, a panic occurred on the New York stock market, followed by a global economic depression. Although the United States quickly achieved temporary stability, the remaining countries remained trapped in a panic from which they could not extricate themselves. Due to domestic economic difficulties and the breakdown of international coordination, the instability of the gold standard, such as the suspension of gold coin convertibility and the restriction or prohibition of gold exports, became a common practice in the past three or four years. The wave even affected other hard currency standards, which also experienced suspensions. According to statistics, there are a total of seventy-four major standard currencies worldwide. At the beginning of this year, only nine maintained a hard currency standard, of which six were on the gold standard: the United States, the Union of South Africa, France, Switzerland, Danzig, and the Netherlands. Three were on the silver standard: China, Persia, and Hong Kong. Recently, the gold standard in the United States has, in fact, been suspended. Although the Washington government has declared that it will maintain the gold standard, gold coin convertibility has already been suspended, and gold exports have been prohibited. Even if one wants to say it has not been suspended, it is impossible. Currently, France, the Netherlands, and others have increased their gold reserves. Optimists believe that the world's fragile gold standard can still be restored, but considering the future of the world economy, its peril is difficult to express. This is truly a major transformation unseen since 1816.

▲ The Flight and Hoarding of Gold

Many commentators attribute the instability of the gold standard to the flight and hoarding of gold. The world's currency in cash was 10,244 million (US dollars) at the end of 1925, 11,052 million at the end of 1928, and 12,078 million at the end of June 1922. The increase rate is indeed not large. Compared to the total volume of global trade at the time, it was insufficient to maintain the original reserve ratio. Among them, the amount held in the United States was 4,399 million at the end of 1925, 4,141 million at the end of 1928, and 4,956 million in June 1931. The amount held in France was 978 million at the end of 1925, 1,271 million at the end of 1928, and 2,212 million in June 1931. The gold reserves of the United States and France increased from about 50% of the world's total to about 60%. This was due to the repatriation of war debts, reparations, and short-term capital from various countries. After the second half of 1931, the United States saw a decrease, while France saw a sharp increase. The majority of the world's gold reserves remained in the hands of these two countries. It is estimated that at the end of 1932, the United States held about 4,500 million dollars, while France exceeded 8.3 million francs. In addition, most other countries experienced a decrease. Japan decreased from 541 million dollars (US dollars) at the end of 1928 to 424 million in June 1931, and even further decreased at the end of 1932, with only 425 million yen. Germany decreased from 676 million dollars (US dollars) at the end of 1928 to 359 million in June 1931, and even further decreased in 1932, with only 79 million marks. The United Kingdom remained relatively stable, but the amount was not large, with 814 million dollars (US dollars) at the end of 1925, 836 million at the end of 1928, 865 million at the end of June 1931, and 110 million pounds at the end of 1932. From a general perspective, it is undeniable that gold fled to countries such as the United States and France, while Japan, Germany, and the United Kingdom inevitably paled in comparison. The situation was even worse for other countries. The gold standard is based on cash as the main currency. Domestic exchange relies on it, and international clearing also relies on it. This is what is meant by the so-called "canal for connecting international economies." Now, a small number of countries hold huge amounts of gold, while the reserves of most countries are dwindling. How can the gold standard of these majority countries be maintained? At a time when the world's gold production is declining, there is also a flight of gold, which is truly a misfortune for the gold standard.

It is already alarming that international gold reserves are not evenly distributed but form a pattern of flight. However, it would still be acceptable if this fleeing gold flowed into useful channels. Unfortunately, those who receive this gold mostly hoard it, thus further reducing its effectiveness and further endangering the foundation of the gold standard. According to statistics, since 1928, the gold reserve ratio of the United States and France has consistently exceeded their paper currency circulation. The gold reserve ratio of the twelve Federal Reserve Banks in the United States was 61.5% of the Federal Reserve notes and deposits at the end of 1928, 69.6% at the end of 1929, and even exceeded 70% in 1930. It gradually decreased afterward, but still reached 61.9% at the end of 1931. The gold reserve ratio of the Bank of France was 79.9% of the banknotes and deposits at the end of 1928 and 80.9% at the end of 1931. The former exceeded the legal reserve ratio by about one-third, while the latter exceeded the legal reserve ratio by more than one time. Therefore, in the United States and France, there is a lot of gold that is hoarded, and social credit does not become active due to the increase in gold. The currency on the market also does not increase due to the abundance of gold reserves. In other words, the currency under their gold standard does not expand or contract with the actual gold reserves. The effectiveness of the gold standard is thus limited. As for other countries, since their gold has already fled, the credit and currency that have historically been based on the gold standard will inevitably develop flaws, gradually leading to a global financial crunch, falling prices, and economic panic. This has been the case for the past three or four years. Commentators often attribute the instability of the gold standard to the flight and hoarding of gold, and there is good reason for this.

▲ Is the Global Economic Panic a Cause or an Effect?

Based on the previous discussion, the instability of the gold standard seems to be due to the flight and hoarding of gold. But is the global economic panic a cause or an effect? This is something that must be discussed. Some say that under the credit system of the gold standard, the expansion and contraction of credit are measured by gold reserves. In recent years, gold has experienced flight and hoarding, and most countries have seen a decrease in gold reserves. With less gold, credit tightens, finance becomes congested, prices fall, and economic panic arises. Albert Tanssen, Reginald Mant, Henry Strakosch, and others all advocate this view. They believe that countries must repay war debts and reparations to the United States and France, leading to a trend of gold flight. After 1928, the United States and France not only did not release funds to other countries but also recovered other debts, further unevenly distributing global gold. The world economy inevitably fell into panic. The report of the League of Nations Gold Committee elaborates on this. This view considers the instability of the gold standard to be the cause of the global economic panic. Others say that since the end of the European War, the economic policies of various countries have undergone a new transformation. The international division of labor before the war has gradually been abandoned, and national capitalism has increasingly risen. Those who preside over a country's economic policies initially strive for self-sufficiency in their own country's raw materials and products, imposing various restrictions on imports. Subsequently, they also strive to dump goods abroad, seeking the prosperity of their own country's industries. Therefore, the production equipment of various countries has expanded, fixed capital has increased, and protective tariffs have been pursued, becoming even more intense in recent years. According to a report from the US Department of Commerce, European countries generally raised tax rates more than six times in the single year of 1930, and Latin American countries generally raised tax rates a total of five times. Gradually, high barriers were erected between countries, and what began as mutual dumping ended in mutual stagnation. International trade greatly declined. Here is a list of the trade of forty-eight countries around the world in the first half of each year (unit: million marks):

1928 1931 1932

Imports 64.1 41.6 27.5

Exports 57.1 36.1 23.7

Total 121.2 77.8 51.2

With the decline of international trade and the obstruction of foreign sales channels, the production equipment of various countries has also become idle assets, and skilled workers have lost their jobs one after another. Economic panic has become a widespread phenomenon. Debtor countries, lacking new international loans to offset their debts to creditor countries such as the United States and France, have no choice but to transport cash, leading to the flight of gold and the eventual collapse of the gold standard. This view considers economic panic to be the cause and the instability of the gold standard to be the effect.

The above two views have completely different causal concepts, and the latter view is more reasonable. Since a fierce tariff war has occurred between various countries, the world economy has lost its interconnectivity. Moreover, the production equipment within each country has been excessively expanded, and the government lacks the ability to implement "controlled economy." Although individual factories and companies have become more scientific and rational, the entire country has become more unscientific and irrational. Under this type of economic organization, how can panic be avoided? Since the signs of a global economic panic have already appeared, currency and finance should naturally be unstable. Moreover, with the recent unevenness of international lending and the flight of gold, the instability of the gold standard is naturally a common cash flow.

▲ The United States Reaps What It Sows

The United States was originally a debtor country. Although its land is vast and its resources are abundant, it did not have much influence in global finance. After the European War, its position changed dramatically. Its foreign claims increased daily, and the power of the gold dollar kingdom shook the globe. Wall Street's replacement of Lombard Street as the center of world finance has lasted for nearly twenty years. In the past four or five years, its massive gold reserves have been even more alarming. Since last year, a tendency of decreasing reserves has begun to appear. If it could make good use of its position to promote the interconnection of the world economy, it might not be without promise. Unfortunately, it has adopted a policy of exploitation toward various countries, while simultaneously increasing protective tariffs and expanding production equipment, fearing to fall behind. As a result, the world economy has declined, exports have sharply decreased, and its domestic market has first experienced a crunch. In the past year, it has even seen an outflow of cash, causing increasing tremors in the hearts of its people and forming the recent panic. Although its gold reserves are still large, panic has already arisen, and people's hearts are wavering, which cannot be calmed by these reserves. Its gold standard has had to be suspended. To put it bluntly, it can be said to have reaped what it sowed. Some say that one of the causes of the US panic is the failure to recover war debts as scheduled. This statement is not unreasonable. However, even if war debts were recovered as scheduled, it would only be enough to form the current surplus. With other countries becoming increasingly impoverished due to debt repayment, the global economic panic would inevitably deepen, US foreign trade would inevitably become more sluggish, and its production capital would inevitably become more idle. Even if it wanted to avoid panic, could it? The eventual instability of its gold standard is both a matter of reason and necessity. Moreover, in recent years, the rise in gold prices seems on the surface to be caused by the flight of gold, but in reality, there are two other reasons: (1) The hoarding of gold. The United States and France hold the most gold but use it the least. In other words, they are most unwilling to rely on gold reserves to expand their credit and promote the activity of currency and finance. The United States did not consider issuing government paper money until the recent panic. If this measure had been taken earlier, the bank's gold reserves would inevitably have decreased due to circulation in the market, but the current panic might have been alleviated. (2) The artificial raising of prices. The United States, with the most gold reserves, would purchase gold whenever gold prices fell, fearing that it would be detrimental to itself. Therefore, a large amount of gold has been collected in the United States. Unexpectedly, holding a lot of gold would lead to idle capital and the eventual occurrence of panic. The recent instability of its gold standard can be said to be reaping what it sowed. The United States now seems to be using a policy of monetary inflation as the backbone of its relief efforts. This is a commonly used method in economic history, but it can only be effective for a short time. Without other effective reorganization methods following it, we ultimately do not believe it is reliable. In this autumn of global economic gloom, can the US panic be stabilized immediately? Can its gold standard ultimately avoid instability? Gazing at the Statue of Liberty, one cannot help but feel pessimistic.

▲ What About France?

The United States and France are the two major gold countries of today. The United States has unfortunately experienced a breakdown, while France has managed to maintain its solid reputation. This can be said to be a highlight for the gold standard. However, there are still two facts that must be explored: (1) The global economic downturn has been prolonged since 1929. With the various barriers between countries, a recovery is difficult to achieve immediately. France's foreign trade, like that of other countries, has declined. Its domestic productivity has also declined. However, the degree of decline is relatively mild. If the industrial production index in 1928 was 100, then the United States was 74.8 in June 1931 and 54.1 in August 1932, while France was 99.2 in June 1931 and 73.2 in August 1932. France is also an industrialized country, with a fairly large-scale production equipment. Given its past downward trend and the current state of the world economy, the outlook for its domestic economy is not optimistic. (2) France's gold reserve ratio to currency circulation is even higher than that of the United States. The expansion of the gold reserve ratio is not inherently a bad phenomenon, but hoarding too much without knowing how to use it is inevitably uneconomical. If it does not use this to expand credit and promote the smooth operation of the world economy, it may not be a blessing for France. The famous French economist Charles Rist once said that the lack of credit expansion is due to the economic downturn, so that banks cannot expand credit even if they want to. This statement has considerable truth. When the economy is depressed, industries are in decline, and banks, for the sake of prudence, find it even more difficult to grant loans. However, in fact, it is only difficult, and the number of those who need funds for reorganization is not small. Considering the increase in the reserve funds of major British banks and the decrease in loans before the panic in the United Kingdom in 1895, one cannot help but worry about France.

In summary, in this tide of global panic, whether the French economy can remain stable and whether its gold standard can avoid instability depends on the actions of various countries. If international coordination cannot be achieved and countries cannot implement controlled economic management, then the world economy will be difficult to recover, and France will not be optimistic. Even if France can maintain its gold standard, the global instability of the gold standard is undoubtedly certain. However, based on the current phenomenon, France's cash reserves are increasing, which may be a good temporary phenomenon for its local situation.

Causes of the American Financial Crisis 215

— Mao Zhenchu

This sudden American financial crisis is like a violent storm descending from the sky, the reason for which is unknown. However, if we analyze the recent domestic economic, social, and political phenomena in the United States, we can understand that the occurrence of this crisis has its own inevitable result.

(1) (Invalidation of Debt) Originally, the prosperity of the United States was a gift of fortune during the European war. Before the war, the United States was the world's largest debtor nation. After the war, it took advantage of the lack of production capacity in various countries to develop its export trade as much as possible. Tracing back to 1915 (the year after the start of the Great War), its foreign trade volume had jumped from 1.4 billion yuan to 2.8 billion yuan, exactly doubling. The following year, as the European war was in full swing, the United States exported large quantities of food and munitions to Europe, further jumping to 5 billion yuan, almost doubling again. In 1920 (two years after the armistice), European countries were still unable to produce due to their devastation. At this time, the total value of US foreign trade reached a record high of 8.2 billion yuan. During these six years, so much money flowed into the United States from foreign countries that it goes without saying that it transformed from poverty to prosperity. However, after this, on the one hand, European cash gradually dried up, and all transactions with the United States could only be done with "debt claims" besides cash. On the other hand, their production capacity also gradually recovered, and US export trade gradually decreased accordingly. The US revenue from foreign money became increasingly scarce. Even if there was any revenue, it was nothing more than debt claims on paper. At the same time, the debt directly issued by the United States to countries such as Britain and France due to the war amounted to more than 10 billion yuan. The repayment of this war debt entirely depended on whether Germany could fulfill its indemnity obligations to Britain and France. Currently, Germany is unable to pay its reparations, which affects the credit of Britain and France in repaying the US war debt, creating a chain of deadlock. The ultimate victim is the United States, which holds the world's debt claims. Therefore, strictly speaking, the prosperity of the United States had already shown a hollow phenomenon since 1921. Its prosperity was built on debt claims, and when debts could not be recovered, the national finance would inevitably fall into a state of financial difficulties. In 1929, there was a stock market boom. It is no wonder that four years later, today, a panic finally occurred due to the lack of settlement of debt claims.

(2) (Financial Deficits) The amount of annual expenditure in the United States' finances was only around one billion before the war, but it jumped to more than four billion after the war. Of the three billion increase, about one-third was the cost of bearing the national debt. During the Great War, the United States' war expenses consumed more than 44 billion yuan, most of which came from issuing national debt. In 1919, the highest amount of national debt could be as much as 25.5 billion yuan. Repaying the principal and interest annually was naturally difficult. In terms of revenue, customs duties accounted for about 600 million yuan, and other sources were income tax, etc. However, the taxes on tobacco, alcohol, and wine, which were the main sources of revenue before the war, underwent complete changes after the war. In particular, the alcohol tax was drastically reduced by about 40 million after the implementation of prohibition. Income tax, etc., also decreased abnormally. At the same time, military spending in 1926 was still 16%, but in 1930, it expanded to 20%. Last year's fiscal year (1931 fiscal year) military expenditure budget was as high as 814,274,000 yuan. It can be seen that in the United States' finances, the tax revenue on the income side has a tendency to decrease sharply year by year, while the huge national debt expenses and military expenditures borne on the expenditure side increase every year. Therefore, since 1931, there has been a state of being stretched thin. In recent years, the most important topic of each parliamentary session has been how to fill the financial deficit. The imbalance between the revenue and expenditure of the national treasury inevitably reduces the credibility of the bonds issued by the country, directly affecting the financial sector, which uses bonds as reserves.

(3) (Trade Depression) Since the European war, the foreign trade of the United States can be roughly divided into three periods. From 1915 to 1921, it can be said to be the golden age; from 1922 to 1929, it was the period of decline; and from 1930 to 1932, it was the period of depression. Its golden age was actually due to the lack of products caused by the European war, and its decline was also due to the fact that European countries were able to produce on their own, and exports decreased accordingly. As for the phenomenon of depression since 1930, it was entirely affected by the world panic. According to statistics, the United States' foreign trade in the past three years has decreased by about one-third compared with 1929. However, 1929 had already entered a period of decline. Therefore, all those with knowledge are worried about it. Some even say that if this state is maintained for a long time, by September 1933, the United States' foreign trade will be completely eliminated. Although this is somewhat of an exaggeration, the degree of this depression can be imagined. The increase or decrease of US foreign trade is closely related to commissions, profits, and employment issues. It is said that at least 2.4 million families in the United States depend on foreign trade for a living. Now, all countries are attacked by the "recession," and they are all competing to protect their domestic markets, either by raising tax rates or implementing "allocation systems" (i.e., separately limiting the import quota of each country) to restrict imports, causing US trade to be completely defeated. How can American foreign traders who depend on this for a living not fall into a difficult situation, and also affect the national economy as a whole?

(4) (Production Deterioration) The industrial production volume of various industrial countries affected by the world recession has naturally declined. According to the German Economic Research Institute, the world industrial production index last year, except for Soviet Russia, India, and Japan, has all retreated to the same level as before the war, which is rare in the past decade. Even if 1913 is taken as 100, last year it was 101. Among them, Germany, the United States, and Poland are particularly severe, and the production in the United States is becoming increasingly worse. The industrial sector of the United States has long been shrinking at any time due to the world recession and the sharp decline in trade. Naturally, there is no longer any concern about overproduction. However, the depression of general industries directly affects the losses of various enterprises and the financial difficulties of the financial sector. At the same time, American agriculture has always been known as developed, and wheat, the main component of agricultural products, is also the main commodity for export. Last year, the total US grain production was more than 304 million bushels, but due to the depression of exports, there was a sudden surplus of grain, and the prices of all food products fell sharply. If 1929 is taken as 100, the price of wheat last year was only 56.5, and other products such as corn were only 66.8. The sharp drop in food prices will inevitably bankrupt the entire rural economy, and agricultural panic will occur. According to statistics, the total debt of farmers across the country is about 20 billion yuan, a staggering figure. The severity of the rural panic has reached this extreme. From this point of view, the United States is under dual pressure in terms of production: 1. Sharp decline in industrial production; 2. Overproduction of agricultural products. These two contradictory phenomena shake the entire economic organization, and the financial panic is inevitable.

(5) (Soaring Unemployment) The so-called world panic actually started with the increasing number of unemployed people. In the past, the world regarded the United States as a wealthy nation, but who knew that in recent years, the surge of unemployment has swept across the United States. In January of this year, William Green, president of the American Federation of Labor, declared, "The number of unemployed people in the United States has reached a peak of 11.6 million. After three years of economic and financial panic in the United States, there is no way out for the unemployed." Moreover, according to Newton Baker, chairman of the Public Welfare and Relief Movement Committee, at the end of last December, perhaps a quarter of the people had no income at all and relied on their relatives, friends, and social unemployment funds for their livelihoods. The reasons for unemployment are the sharp decline in industrial production and the overproduction of agricultural products, which can all lead to mass layoffs. Therefore, the number of unemployed people in the United States is the highest in the world, more than double that of Germany, which ranks second with 5 million. Since unemployment is an important factor in promoting panic, the indirect increase in the panic in the forty-eight states by 10 million unemployed people is within our imagination.

The various tragic scenes mentioned above surround the entire American financial sector day and night. The maturity of the conditions for the financial crisis has been waiting to happen. The arrow is on the string, and it will be triggered at any moment. Before today, it was like a machine with all the components in place, but lacking fuel to drive it. And today, the fuel is ready. The so-called fuel is the dishonored withdrawal of 7.5 million yuan in deposits from the Ford Motor Company to the Detroit Union Trust Company, the transition of new and old presidents in politics, the outflow of cash from the banking sector overseas to repay short-term foreign debts, and the sharp drop in stock prices. The recent decline in the US stock market is more severe than in September last year. Railway stocks have decreased by about 39%, and industrial stocks have also decreased by 35%. Since stocks have a close relationship with the banking sector, the sharp decline in stocks has naturally caused the banks' lending and credit to be shaken. The general public is even more aware that the political situation is in a period of transition between new and old presidents, and they all suspect that the new president's ascent to the throne may change important systems such as finance and currency, causing psychological anxiety. Therefore, when they heard the rumor that Ford's withdrawal was dishonored, they took the opportunity to withdraw deposits from banks. And when the banks were in a state of cash emptiness, they caused this huge wave. Some say that Ford Company and the outgoing President Hoover had a considerable relationship, and the withdrawal may have had a political effect. But they did not realize that this kind of behavior harmed others without benefiting oneself, and they would not do this. However, the impact of political changes on people's psychology directly promoted the financial crisis, which is an undeniable fact. Moreover, the rapid promotion of this financial crisis is not without defects in the system of the banks themselves. The US banks are independent systems and do not have branches. The 18,000 major banks in the country are independent and do not support each other. Therefore, when a financial crisis occurs, they often lose their turnover capacity. Unlike banks in the UK, etc., which adopt a branch system, they can use the power of branches in various places to transfer and operate each other, and they will not be forced to close down at every turn.

England After Abandoning the Gold Standard 216

— Shi Chu Tiao

Since the German financial panic broke out on May 12, 1931, shaking the foundations of credit in the British Isles, it has triggered a wave of capital flight from Germany and the repatriation of investments in England by other countries. This intensified the abnormal movement of international gold, forcing England to abandon the gold standard on September 21, 1931, and legally restrict foreign exchange on the 23rd.

However, it has been more than a year and four months since the abandonment of the gold standard. To what extent has it affected the British economy? In fact, the effects on British industry have been minimal, and have not even achieved the results that the British expected. For example, the price of the gold pound fell 10% in the two months after the abandonment. Furthermore, the bold increase in interest rates in the London financial market created an "unprecedented" phenomenon since 1897. However, this unnatural high interest rate was nothing more than the Bank of England trying to prevent inflation and desperately restricting the outflow of money, which led to the fact that the amount of paper currency in circulation could not increase as before. At the same time, as a result of rising prices, a huge amount of capital was needed. In other words, the result of abandoning the gold standard was that it was necessary to increase capital, and at the same time, because of fear of inflation, interest rates had to be raised.

Regarding the cost of living for the people, according to a survey by the British government's Ministry of Labour, it has not been expensive since September, when the gold standard was abandoned. On the contrary, wholesale prices have risen by more than 10% during this period. Furthermore, it is not only raw materials, but also domestic and foreign goods. Furthermore, the wholesale prices of domestic food and raw materials also rose by an average of 5% to 10% in the two months after the abandonment. In addition, the rate of increase in the price of imported raw materials is not much different from that of domestic products. Retail prices have not risen because the general wages and rents at that time were the same as before and had not increased.

In addition, due to the impact of the fall in the gold pound, the prices of its exports were also 20% lower than before. However, it is still doubtful whether the UK can regain the market it lost after the European war due to the fall in the gold pound and prices.

In fact, although the total amount of British foreign trade has made slight progress since the abandonment of the gold standard, the amount is still very small. Imports have only increased slightly due to seasonal factors or increased tariffs, but the increase in exports is very small. Let's look at the following table to understand.

British Trade Volume with Prohibition of Gold Exports in 1931

Imports　　　Exports　　　Trade Deficit

August　　　　　65.3　　　33.0　　　32.3

September　　　68.3　　　33.6　　　34.7

October　　　　　80.7　　　38.1　　　42.6

November　　　83.2　　　36.8　　　46.4

However, in the two months after the abandonment, the number of unemployed people decreased by 150,000. During this period, the number of unemployed people should have been constantly increasing, but why could it be reduced as a result? That is because, as shown in the table above, during these four months, British foreign trade had increased from 33 million pounds to 36.8 million pounds. From this we can know that the scope of the decrease in unemployed people is by no means common to all industrial sectors, but only belongs to the export industrial sector.

As for solving the gold pound problem, the British government suddenly abandoned the gold standard and prohibited gold exports as a last resort and a temporary measure; it was by no means a permanent laissez-faire policy. Now, although the discussions on this issue are different, there are three main opinions. The content of these three opinions is briefly described below:

The first opinion is to make the price of the gold pound fall, that is, to make the price of the ordinary gold pound cheaper than before; however, on the other hand, the general prices and wages are the same as before and do not increase or decrease. This is the simplest main opinion of the British Labour Party. Today, there are many people in the British economic sector who agree with this view.

The second opinion is to seek flexibility in gold prices through international coordination. The main points of its advocacy are: when the economy is in recession, the exchange rate should be cheaper than usual, and use this to stimulate general industrial sectors and export sectors. As for the method, it strives to coordinate with the world's major powers. In particular, it hopes to conclude some kind of agreement with the US reserve banks, which account for more than half of the world's gold, to prevent gold prices from skyrocketing.

Although this opinion is extremely ingenious and ideal, it is difficult to carry out in recent years. Because the gold countries such as the United States or France have already solved the difficulties in their own countries when this economic panic is prevalent in the world, how can they still have the energy to help England? This opinion is advocated by the famous British economist Keynes (J. M. Keyens), and many people agree with this view.

The third opinion is to seek to combine the market price of the gold pound with the price index and to balance the changes between the two. Its proponent is the manager of the Bank of England, Sir B. Blackelt. Because the Puxi faction has always been known for challenging "gold autocracy," and wants to harmonize the value of currency with the average market price of goods, so as to replace the gold standard currency and set a currency based on the price index, its purpose is nothing more than to stabilize prices.

Among the above three opinions, the third opinion is quite powerful. However, in the future, the gold pound will not exist to regulate the value of gold; it is bound to regulate the average price of many commodities in the name of the gold pound.

In short, the common goal of the above three opinions is to stabilize prices within the economic region of the British Empire. In other words, the British economic sector, since the abandonment of the gold standard, has been working hard to solve the gold pound problem, and their common conclusion is to abolish the gold standard monetary system and establish a price index-based monetary system; at the same time, this kind of index-based monetary system is the only way out for the British Empire.

Two Reforms in the Gold Exchange 218

▲Change to Using Dollar Standard…Correcting Rollover Date▲

Starting from this rollover (16th), there will be two reforms in the Gold Industry Exchange. One is to implement the abolition of taels and the change to dollars, which has been clearly announced. The other is to correct the early rollover before the specified date. Although this matter was proposed by the brokers, it has not yet been officially decided. Now, the situation is recorded below:

(1) The Gold Exchange Implements the Use of Dollar Standard The Gold Exchange issued a notice yesterday, which stated: "According to the official letter from the supervisor, in compliance with the order of the Ministry of Finance, from the May trading onwards, all bid prices and fund inflows and outflows will be calculated in silver dollars. The handling fee (commission) for each gold bar is 2.1 li in silver dollars, excluding the broker's bonus, the actual charge is 1 fen, 5 li and 7.5 hao in silver dollars. All transactions in March and April, which were originally calculated in customs taels, will be converted to silver dollar prices in accordance with the regulations (715) at the time of this rollover. The rollover transaction should use silver dollar yuan and jiao as the price. The asking price is in units of 1 jiao in silver dollars."

(2) Correcting the Rollover Date The brokers have made this proposal, and the reason is quite justified. Because the Exchange has always had the habit of starting the rollover one day in advance during the rollover. If the official listing on the next day differs too much, customers often complain. Therefore, it is proposed that every time before the rollover, rollover trading should start from 2:00 pm on the day before, and rollover trading prices should be added. This case has been submitted to the Brokers Association and has been passed, but it will be implemented from the next session (because the time is short and the procedures are not completed this month on the 16th)."

Securities: Bond Market Safely Passed Through the Stormy Waves Last Week 219

Last week, from March 6th to 11th, the China Merchants Securities Exchange, the bond market, after the entire observation, can be called a good week. Although there were many changes in the situation, such as the loss of Rehe, the crisis in Tianjin, and the departure of Zhang from the North, etc., the price movement was like a boat sailing through stormy waves, and it safely passed through. Onlookers on land were extremely frightened. In the harsh environment, the price rose against the norm, and the reasons for this are roughly the following four points:

(Related to the war) The gains and losses of Rehe were already expected by speculators and were not related to their interests. Although the situation in Tianjin was critical, it was still a feint by the Japanese, a threatening move. Moreover, the authorities were extremely well prepared, and there would not be any changes in a short time. Retail speculation, subjective mistakes, must be made up after being shorted, which is enough to help the bond market rise.

(Related to transactions) The biggest reason for the rise and fall of the bond market is the comparison of the strength of the long and short sides. The one with strong strength naturally has the advantage. At this time, most of the long positions in the transaction accounts belonged to powerful figures, while most of the short positions were retail investors. The long side remained unchanged from beginning to end, and the short side took the situation as its goal. At first, it insisted, but eventually it relaxed. Supply was difficult to obtain, and the price was naturally not easy to fall.

(Related to the financial authorities) The financial authorities' financial management methods have reversed the previous policy of excessively issuing public bonds and draining the pond to catch fish. Since 1921, no new public bonds in circulation have been issued, so the chips are gradually lacking. Those who hold spot goods have learned from the fall after the September 18th Incident and the rise after the January 28th Incident. They have learned their lessons and are unwilling to sell easily, which is also one of the reasons for helping to rise.

(Related to the money market) Since the war in the northeast was fierce, rumors started in Pingjin, and cash in the north gradually concentrated in Shanghai. There was a surplus of silver and investment was difficult. Buying bonds to generate interest was more appropriate and profitable. This kind of collection was also considerable, and circulation in the market gradually became scarce. This kind of boost also had a role to play.

Looking at the above four points, before there are major changes in the mainland, the long side's defenses are strong and not easy to shake. Therefore, although there were not many transactions last week, except for Monday and Thursday in June, when the loss of Rehe and Zhang's departure from the North, new short positions joined the battle, and the market price slightly retraced a few corners. The remaining four days were gradually rising. In particular, when Chairman Chiang Kai-shek personally went north to supervise the war on Tuesday, the people were greatly encouraged, and the biggest increase was about one and a half yuan. As a result of the whole week, the increase ranged from a few corners to one yuan. The salt tax, at the 40 yuan mark, fluctuated several times, and the result was still closing at 4000 yuan. The process was very good. The total transaction volume was 46,735,000 yuan.

Silk and Tea 224

Two batches of artificial silk ordered by inland silk merchants have been shipped to Shanghai

Due to the need for silk fabrics in the spring and summer seasons, inland manufacturers have ordered a large quantity of artificial silk of various thicknesses from various countries through artificial silk firms in Shanghai. In addition to the previous shipment of over 1,700 boxes on the Italian postal ship "Kenqi," the Italian ship "Kangtuo Fute" this time carried over 1,300 boxes, of which over 700 boxes were ordered by Chinese merchants. This is the second large batch of artificial silk shipped to Shanghai this year and is currently stored in Customs Warehouses No. 3 and No. 5.
